  <script>
  (function(){
    const dropzone   = document.getElementById('bgDropzone');
    const fileInput  = document.getElementById('bgFileInput');
    const fileChip   = document.getElementById('bgFileChip');
    const removeBtn  = document.getElementById('bgRemoveBtn');
    const errorEl    = document.getElementById('bgError');
    const origImg    = document.getElementById('bgOrigImg');
    const resultImg  = document.getElementById('bgResultImg');
    const previews   = document.getElementById('bgPreviews');
    const emptyEl    = document.getElementById('bgEmpty');
    const dlBtn      = document.getElementById('bgDownloadBtn');
    const stageLabel = document.getElementById('bgStageLabel');
    const resultWrap = document.getElementById('bgResultWrap');

    let currentFile = null;
    let selectedFill = 'transparent';

    // remove.bg key field
    (function initBgKeyField() {
      const field = document.getElementById('bgKeyField');
      const saveBtn = document.getElementById('bgKeySaveBtn');
      const dot = document.getElementById('bgKeyDot');
      function mask(key) { return key ? key.slice(0,4) + '••••••••' + key.slice(-4) : ''; }
      function refresh() {
        const key = getRemoveBgKey();
        field.value = mask(key);
        dot.className = key ? 'gm-key-dot2 ok' : 'gm-key-dot2';
      }
      field.addEventListener('focus', () => { if (getRemoveBgKey() && field.value.includes('••')) field.value = ''; });
      field.addEventListener('blur', () => { if (!field.value && getRemoveBgKey()) field.value = mask(getRemoveBgKey()); });
      saveBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const raw = field.value.trim();
        if (!raw || raw.includes('••')) return;
        localStorage.setItem('bg_apikey_removebg', raw);
        refresh();
      });
      refresh();
    })();

    // Dropzone
    dropzone.addEventListener('click', () => fileInput.click());
    dropzone.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); dropzone.classList.add('drag'); });
    dropzone.addEventListener('dragleave', () => dropzone.classList.remove('drag'));
    dropzone.addEventListener('drop', e => { e.preventDefault(); dropzone.classList.remove('drag'); handleFile(e.dataTransfer.files[0]); });
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', () => handleFile(fileInput.files[0]));

    function handleFile(f) {
      if (!f || !f.type.startsWith('image/')) return;
      currentFile = f;
      fileChip.innerHTML = '<div class="file-chip"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" width="14" height="14"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><circle cx="9" cy="9" r="1.8"/><path d="M21 15l-5-5L5 21"/></svg><span class="name">' + f.name + '</span><span class="clear" id="bgClearFile">×</span></div>';
      document.getElementById('bgClearFile').onclick = () => { currentFile = null; fileChip.innerHTML = ''; removeBtn.disabled = true; };
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = e => { origImg.src = e.target.result; };
      reader.readAsDataURL(f);
      removeBtn.disabled = false;
      errorEl.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // Fill color buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.bg-color-btn').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('.bg-color-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        btn.classList.add('active');
        selectedFill = btn.dataset.fill;
        applyFillToResult();
      });
    });
    document.getElementById('bgCustomColor').addEventListener('input', e => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.bg-color-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      selectedFill = e.target.value;
      applyFillToResult();
    });

    function applyFillToResult() {
      if (selectedFill === 'transparent') {
        resultWrap.style.background = '';
        resultWrap.className = 'bg-checkerboard bg-result-wrap';
      } else {
        resultWrap.style.background = selectedFill;
        resultWrap.className = 'bg-result-wrap';
      }
    }

    removeBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      if (!currentFile) return;
      const removeBgKey = getRemoveBgKey();
      if (!removeBgKey) { showError('Add your remove.bg key above first (get a free one at remove.bg/api).'); return; }

      setLoading(true);
      errorEl.style.display = 'none';
      stageLabel.textContent = 'processing…';

      try {
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('image_file', currentFile);
        formData.append('size', 'auto');

        const res = await fetch('https://api.remove.bg/v1.0/removebg', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'X-Api-Key': removeBgKey },
          body: formData
        });

        if (!res.ok) {
          const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
          showError('remove.bg error: ' + (err.errors?.[0]?.title || res.status));
          setLoading(false); return;
        }

        const blob = await res.blob();
        const url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        resultImg.src = url;
        dlBtn.href = url;
        dlBtn.style.display = 'flex';

        emptyEl.style.display = 'none';
        previews.style.display = 'flex';
        applyFillToResult();
        stageLabel.textContent = currentFile.name + ' — background removed';
      } catch(err) {
        showError('Network error: ' + err.message);
        stageLabel.textContent = 'error';
      }
      setLoading(false);
    });

    function setLoading(on) {
      if (on) {
        removeBtn.disabled = true;
        removeBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="bg-spinner"></span> Removing…';
      } else {
        removeBtn.disabled = false;
        removeBtn.innerHTML = '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="14" height="14"><path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4h8v2M19 6l-1 14H6L5 6"/></svg> Remove Background';
      }
    }

    function showError(msg) {
      errorEl.textContent = msg;
      errorEl.style.display = 'block';
      stageLabel.textContent = 'error';
    }
  })();
  </script>
</div>

  <script>
  (function(){
    /* ── DOM refs ── */
    const dropzone    = document.getElementById('ffDropzone');
    const fileInput   = document.getElementById('ffFileInput');
    const findBtn     = document.getElementById('ffFindBtn');
    const errorEl     = document.getElementById('ffError');
    const resultsBody = document.getElementById('ffResultsBody');
    const progressEl  = document.getElementById('ffProgress');
    const resultsLabel= document.getElementById('ffResultsLabel');
    const previewText = document.getElementById('ffPreviewText');
    const sizeSlider  = document.getElementById('ffSizeSlider');
    const sizeVal     = document.getElementById('ffSizeVal');
    const keyStatus   = document.getElementById('ffKeyStatus');
    const serverDot   = document.getElementById('ffServerDot');
    const serverText  = document.getElementById('ffServerText');
    const FONT_SERVER_URL = 'http://127.0.0.1:5001';
    const filterRow   = document.getElementById('ffFilterRow');
    const histSection = document.getElementById('ffHistSection');
    const histEl      = document.getElementById('ffHistory');
    const modeHint    = document.getElementById('ffModeHint');
    const heroEl      = document.getElementById('ffHero');
    const workspaceEl = document.getElementById('ffWorkspace');
    const workThumb   = document.getElementById('ffWorkThumb');
    const changeBtn   = document.getElementById('ffChangeBtn');
    const settingsBtn = document.getElementById('ffSettingsBtn');
    const settingsPop = document.getElementById('ffSettingsPop');

    let currentB64   = null;
    let currentMime  = 'image/jpeg';
    let currentDataUrl = null;
    let detailLevel  = 'quick';
    let resultCount  = 3;
    let allFonts     = [];
    let previewFontSize = 28;

    const MODE_HINTS = {
      quick: 'Quick scan — best match for the dominant font.',
      deep:  'Deep analysis — 6 candidates with detailed letterform reasoning.',
      multi: 'Multi-font detect — identifies all distinct fonts in the image.'
    };

    /* ── Hero / workspace state ── */
    function showHero() {
      heroEl.style.display = '';
      workspaceEl.style.display = 'none';
      currentB64 = null; currentDataUrl = null;
      findBtn.disabled = true;
      fileInput.value = '';
      resetResults();
    }
    function showWorkspace() {
      heroEl.style.display = 'none';
      workspaceEl.style.display = 'block';
    }
    changeBtn.addEventListener('click', showHero);

    /* ── Settings popover ── */
    settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', e => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      settingsPop.classList.toggle('open');
      settingsBtn.classList.toggle('active');
    });
    document.addEventListener('click', e => {
      if (!settingsPop.contains(e.target) && e.target !== settingsBtn) {
        settingsPop.classList.remove('open');
        settingsBtn.classList.remove('active');
      }
    });

    /* ── Font server status ── */
    let serverConnected = false;
    let serverEverConnected = false;
    function setServerStatus(ok, detail) {
      serverConnected = ok;
      serverDot.style.background = ok ? 'var(--ff-good)' : 'var(--ff-warn)';
      serverText.textContent = detail;
    }
    async function checkFontServer() {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`${FONT_SERVER_URL}/status`, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(2500) });
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          serverEverConnected = true;
          setServerStatus(!!data.configured,
            data.configured ? 'Connected — ready to identify fonts' : 'Connected, but ANTHROPIC_API_KEY is not set on the server');
          return;
        }
        setServerStatus(false, 'Font server responded with an error');
      } catch (err) {
        setServerStatus(false, serverEverConnected
          ? 'Font server stopped — its terminal window was likely closed'
          : 'Not running — start it with: python font_server.py');
      }
    }
    checkFontServer();
    setInterval(checkFontServer, 8000);

    /* ── Mode chips ── */
    document.getElementById('ffModeRow').addEventListener('click', e => {
      const chip = e.target.closest('.ff-mode-chip');
      if (!chip) return;
      document.querySelectorAll('.ff-mode-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
      chip.classList.add('active');
      detailLevel = chip.dataset.detail;
      resultCount = parseInt(chip.dataset.count) || 3;
      modeHint.textContent = MODE_HINTS[detailLevel] || '';
    });

    /* ── Preview text & size ── */
    previewText.addEventListener('input', () => {
      document.querySelectorAll('.ff-preview-text').forEach(el => {
        el.textContent = previewText.value || 'The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog';
      });
    });
    sizeSlider.addEventListener('input', () => {
      previewFontSize = parseInt(sizeSlider.value);
      sizeVal.textContent = previewFontSize + 'px';
      document.querySelectorAll('.ff-preview-text').forEach(el => {
        el.style.fontSize = previewFontSize + 'px';
      });
    });

    /* ── Filter chips ── */
    document.getElementById('ffFilterRow').addEventListener('click', e => {
      const chip = e.target.closest('.ff-filter-chip');
      if (!chip) return;
      document.querySelectorAll('.ff-filter-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
      chip.classList.add('active');
      const f = chip.dataset.filter;
      document.querySelectorAll('.ff-card').forEach(card => {
        card.style.display = (f === 'all' || card.dataset.category === f) ? '' : 'none';
      });
    });

    /* ── Drop zone — click, drag-and-drop, and file-dialog ── */
    // Click anywhere on the dropzone → open file picker
    dropzone.addEventListener('click', e => {
      if (e.target === fileInput) return;
      fileInput.value = '';              // reset so same file can be re-selected
      fileInput.click();
    });
    fileInput.addEventListener('click', e => e.stopPropagation());

    // Drag over dropzone (and whole sidebar) → highlight
    function onDragEnter(e) {
      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
      dropzone.classList.add('drag');
    }
    function onDragLeave(e) {
      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
      // Only remove highlight when leaving the dropzone itself (not child elements)
      if (!dropzone.contains(e.relatedTarget)) dropzone.classList.remove('drag');
    }
    function onDragOver(e) {
      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
      e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'copy';
      dropzone.classList.add('drag');
    }
    function onDrop(e) {
      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
      dropzone.classList.remove('drag');
      const f = (e.dataTransfer.files && e.dataTransfer.files[0])
             || (e.dataTransfer.items && e.dataTransfer.items[0] && e.dataTransfer.items[0].kind === 'file'
                 ? e.dataTransfer.items[0].getAsFile() : null);
      if (f) handleFile(f);
    }

    // Attach to both the dropzone div AND the whole page so dropping anywhere on the
    // Font Finder tab works
    const ffPage = document.getElementById('page-fontfinder');
    [dropzone, ffPage].forEach(el => {
      el.addEventListener('dragenter', onDragEnter);
      el.addEventListener('dragover',  onDragOver);
      el.addEventListener('dragleave', onDragLeave);
      el.addEventListener('drop',      onDrop);
    });

    // File dialog → change event
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', () => {
      const f = fileInput.files && fileInput.files[0];
      if (f) handleFile(f);
      fileInput.value = ''; // reset so same file re-triggers change
    });

    /* Prevent browser from navigating away when file is dropped outside the zone */
    document.addEventListener('dragover', e => e.preventDefault());
    document.addEventListener('drop', e => e.preventDefault());

    /* Paste */
    document.addEventListener('paste', e => {
      if (!document.getElementById('page-fontfinder').classList.contains('active')) return;
      const items = e.clipboardData?.items;
      if (!items) return;
      for (const item of items) {
        if (item.type.startsWith('image/')) { handleFile(item.getAsFile()); break; }
      }
    });

    function handleFile(f) {
      if (!f) return;
      // Some browsers/OS send empty MIME on drag-drop — fall back by extension
      const mime = f.type || (
        /\.png$/i.test(f.name) ? 'image/png' :
        /\.jpe?g$/i.test(f.name) ? 'image/jpeg' :
        /\.webp$/i.test(f.name) ? 'image/webp' :
        /\.gif$/i.test(f.name) ? 'image/gif' : ''
      );
      if (!mime.startsWith('image/')) {
        errorEl.textContent = 'Please drop an image file (PNG, JPG, WEBP).';
        errorEl.style.display = 'block';
        return;
      }
      currentMime = mime;
      errorEl.style.display = 'none';
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = ev => {
        currentDataUrl = ev.target.result;
        currentB64 = ev.target.result.split(',')[1];
        workThumb.src = currentDataUrl;
        findBtn.disabled = false;
        resultsLabel.textContent = 'Image ready — checking reference database';
        showWorkspace();
        setTimeout(() => findBtn.click(), 250);
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(f);
    }

    /* ── History ── */
    function loadHistory() {
      try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ff_history') || '[]'); } catch { return []; }
    }
    function saveHistory(dataUrl) {
      let h = loadHistory();
      h = [dataUrl, ...h.filter(u => u !== dataUrl)].slice(0, 8);
      localStorage.setItem('ff_history', JSON.stringify(h));
      renderHistory();
    }
    function renderHistory() {
      const h = loadHistory();
      if (!h.length) { histSection.style.display = 'none'; return; }
      histSection.style.display = 'block';
      histEl.innerHTML = '';
      h.forEach(url => {
        const thumb = document.createElement('div');
        thumb.className = 'ff-hist-thumb';
        thumb.innerHTML = '<img src="' + url + '" alt="">';
        thumb.title = 'Re-analyse this image';
        thumb.addEventListener('click', () => {
          currentDataUrl = url;
          currentB64 = url.split(',')[1];
          currentMime = url.startsWith('data:image/png') ? 'image/png' : 'image/jpeg';
          workThumb.src = url;
          findBtn.disabled = false;
          showWorkspace();
          findBtn.click();
        });
        histEl.appendChild(thumb);
      });
    }
    renderHistory();

    /* ── Main find handler ── */
    findBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      if (!currentB64) return;
      setLoading(true);
      errorEl.style.display = 'none';
      resultsLabel.textContent = 'Analysing with Gemini Vision…';
      filterRow.style.display = 'none';
      allFonts = [];

      try {
        const fonts = await analyzeViaServer(currentB64, currentMime, detailLevel, resultCount);
        allFonts = fonts;
        saveHistory(currentDataUrl);
        renderResults(fonts);
        resultsLabel.textContent = fonts.length + ' font' + (fonts.length !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' identified';
        if (fonts.length > 1) filterRow.style.display = 'flex';
      } catch(err) {
        showError('Error: ' + err.message);
        resultsLabel.textContent = 'Analysis failed';
      }
      setLoading(false);
    });

    /* ── Claude API ── */

    /* Build lookup maps for fast matching */
    const FONT_FAMILIES = [...new Set(FONT_REFERENCE_DB.map(f => f.family.toLowerCase()))];
    const FONT_NAMES_FLAT = FONT_REFERENCE_DB.map(f => f.fontName.toLowerCase());

    /**
     * Given a font name returned by Claude, try to find the best match
     * in our reference database and enrich the result with reference data.
     */
    function enrichWithReference(fontResult) {
      const nameLower = (fontResult.name || '').toLowerCase();
      
      // 1. Try exact fontName match
      let match = FONT_REFERENCE_DB.find(f => f.fontName.toLowerCase() === nameLower);
      
      // 2. Try family + style combo
      if (!match) {
        const familyLower = nameLower;
        match = FONT_REFERENCE_DB.find(f => f.family.toLowerCase() === familyLower);
      }
      
      // 3. Try partial family name match
      if (!match) {
        match = FONT_REFERENCE_DB.find(f => 
          nameLower.includes(f.family.toLowerCase()) || 
          f.family.toLowerCase().includes(nameLower.split(' ')[0])
        );
      }

      if (match) {
        return {
          ...fontResult,
          refFontName: match.fontName,
          refFamily: match.family,
          refStyle: match.style,
          refCategory: match.category,
          refFoundry: match.foundry,
          foundInReference: true,
          // Override foundry with reference data if Claude didn't provide it
          foundry: fontResult.foundry || match.foundry,
          category: fontResult.category || match.category,
        };
      }
      return { ...fontResult, foundInReference: false };
    }

    async function analyzeViaServer(b64, mime, detail, count) {
      // Build reference family list from embedded database for prompt context
      const refFamilies = [...new Set(FONT_REFERENCE_DB.map(f => f.family))].join(', ');
      // Shared letterform checklist — forces Claude to actually inspect distinguishing
      // traits instead of pattern-matching to the first plausible font name it thinks of.
      const traitChecklist = `Before naming any font, examine these letterform traits in the image and let them drive your answer:
- Lowercase "a": single-story or double-story
- Lowercase "g": single-story or double-story
- Terminals: cut straight, angled, or rounded (look at "t", "f", "j", "y")
- Aperture: open or closed (look at "c", "e", "s")
- Stroke contrast: uniform (geometric/grotesque) or modulated (humanist/serif)
- x-height: relatively tall/short vs cap-height
- Serifs (if any): bracketed/unbracketed, slab, hairline
- Distinctive characters if visible: "R" leg, "Q" tail, "&", "1", "M" apex/vertex

REFERENCE FONT DATABASE — when letterforms are consistent with a font in this list, prefer naming it exactly:
${refFamilies}

CRITICAL — exact identification vs. visual resemblance:
- Set "isExactMatch": true ONLY if the letterforms are a precise match to a specific named typeface you can identify with high confidence (e.g. unmistakable Helvetica "a"/"t" or distinctive Futura geometric "o").
- Set "isExactMatch": false if you are naming a font because it is stylistically similar (same category, similar trait profile) but you cannot confirm it's that exact cut — this is the common case for generic sans/serif text, and you should say so honestly rather than guessing a specific commercial name.
- Never invent a font name. If genuinely uncertain between 2-3 candidates with similar trait profiles, list them as separate ranked entries rather than picking one and overstating confidence.
- Confidence above 85 should be reserved for cases where isExactMatch is true.`;

      let prompt;
      if (detail === 'multi') {
        prompt = `You are an expert typographer performing forensic font identification. Analyse this image and identify ALL distinct fonts used (different typefaces, not just weights).

${traitChecklist}

Return ONLY a valid JSON array. For each font found, include:
- "name": exact font name
- "category": "Sans-Serif"|"Serif"|"Monospace"|"Display"|"Script"|"Slab-Serif"
- "confidence": integer 1-100
- "isExactMatch": true|false (see rules above)
- "usedFor": what text uses this font (e.g. "headline", "body copy", "logo text")
- "designer": designer name or null
- "foundry": foundry name or null
- "googleFonts": true/false
- "traits": short string of the specific letterform traits observed (e.g. "double-story a/g, closed aperture, uniform stroke")
- "reasoning": specific letterform evidence for this identification, referencing the traits above
- "notes": one-line font character description

Be precise. If only one font is used, return a single-item array.`;
      } else {
        const depthNote = detail === 'deep'
          ? 'Provide detailed reasoning noting specific letterform traits: x-height, terminals, apertures, stroke contrast, axis, spacing — cite the actual characters you examined.'
          : 'Be concise but accurate; still ground your answer in at least one specific letterform trait.';
        prompt = `You are an expert typographer and font identification specialist performing forensic-level analysis. Analyse this image and identify the fonts used.

${traitChecklist}

Return ONLY a valid JSON array with exactly ${count} suggestions ordered by confidence (highest first). Each object:
- "name": exact font name (e.g. "Helvetica Neue", "Playfair Display")
- "category": "Sans-Serif"|"Serif"|"Monospace"|"Display"|"Script"|"Slab-Serif"
- "confidence": integer 1-100
- "isExactMatch": true|false (see rules above)
- "designer": designer name or null
- "foundry": foundry/company or null
- "googleFonts": true if on Google Fonts, false otherwise
- "traits": short string of the specific letterform traits observed (e.g. "single-story a, open aperture, angled terminals")
- "reasoning": why this font matches the letterforms you see — reference specific characters
- "notes": one-line character description (e.g. "Geometric grotesque with uniform strokes")
- "usedFor": null

${depthNote}
Focus on the most prominent typography. No markdown fences, no explanation — JSON only.`;
      }

      let resp;
      try {
        resp = await fetch(`${FONT_SERVER_URL}/find-font`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          signal: AbortSignal.timeout(35000), // give the server's own 30s timeout room to fire first
          body: JSON.stringify({
            image: `data:${mime || 'image/jpeg'};base64,${b64}`,
            mime: mime || 'image/jpeg',
            prompt
          })
        });
      } catch (networkErr) {
        if (networkErr.name === 'TimeoutError' || networkErr.name === 'AbortError') {
          throw new Error(
            `Request timed out after 35s waiting for a response. The font server or Gemini API ` +
            `may be slow, rate-limited, or unreachable — check the terminal running font_server.py for details.`
          );
        }
        // fetch() itself throws (TypeError) when the request can't even reach the
        // server — server not running, wrong port, or the browser blocked the
        // localhost request (Chrome's Private Network Access check can silently
        // block file:// pages from calling http://127.0.0.1 without warning).
        throw new Error(
          `Could not reach font_server.py at ${FONT_SERVER_URL}. Make sure it's running ` +
          `("python font_server.py" — check the terminal for errors), and if you're ` +
          `opening this file directly (file://) try serving it over http://localhost ` +
          `instead, since some browsers block localhost requests from file:// pages.`
        );
      }

      if (!resp.ok) {
        const err = await resp.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new Error(err.error || `Server error ${resp.status}`);
      }
      let parsed;
      try {
        parsed = await resp.json();
      } catch {
        throw new Error('Server returned a response that was not valid JSON.');
      }
      return (Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [parsed]).map(enrichWithReference);
    }

    /* ── Render results ── */
    function renderResults(fonts) {
      // Clear but keep progress ref
      resultsBody.innerHTML = '';
      resultsBody.appendChild(progressEl);
      progressEl.style.display = 'none';

      const GF_BASE = 'https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=';
      const preview = previewText.value || 'The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog';

      fonts.forEach((font, i) => {
        const safeName  = font.name.replace(/ /g, '+');
        const isGF      = font.googleFonts !== false;
        const confColor = font.confidence >= 80 ? 'var(--ff-good)' : font.confidence >= 60 ? 'var(--ff-warn)' : 'var(--ff-accent)';
        const isTop     = i === 0;

        // Load font from Google Fonts if available
        if (isGF && !document.querySelector(`link[data-ff-font="${safeName}"]`)) {
          const link = document.createElement('link');
          link.rel = 'stylesheet';
          link.href = GF_BASE + safeName + ':wght@400;700&display=swap';
          link.dataset.ffFont = safeName;
          document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        const fontStyle = isGF ? `font-family:'${font.name}',serif;` : '';
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'ff-card' + (isTop ? ' top-match' : '');
        card.dataset.category = font.category || '';

        const exactBadge = font.isExactMatch === true
          ? '<span class="ff-badge ff-badge-exact">Exact match</span>'
          : '<span class="ff-badge ff-badge-close">Closest style</span>';
        const metaBits = [
          font.refFamily || font.category || '',
          font.refFoundry || font.foundry || '',
          font.refStyle || font.designer || '',
          font.usedFor ? 'used for ' + font.usedFor : ''
        ].filter(Boolean).join(' · ');

        card.innerHTML = `
          <div class="ff-card-head">
            <span class="ff-card-rank">#${i+1}</span>
            <div class="ff-card-info">
              <div class="ff-card-name">${font.name}</div>
              <div class="ff-card-meta">${metaBits}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="ff-card-badges">
              ${exactBadge}
              ${isGF ? '<span class="ff-badge ff-badge-gf">Google Fonts</span>' : ''}
              ${font.category ? '<span class="ff-badge ff-badge-cat">' + font.category.split('-')[0] + '</span>' : ''}
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="ff-conf-row">
            <div class="ff-conf-bar"><div class="ff-conf-fill" style="width:0%;background:${confColor};" data-width="${font.confidence}"></div></div>
            <span class="ff-conf-pct" style="color:${confColor};">${font.confidence}%</span>
          </div>
          <div class="ff-card-preview">
            <div class="ff-preview-text" style="${fontStyle}font-size:${previewFontSize}px;">${preview}</div>
            ${font.traits ? '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--ff-ink-dim);margin-top:8px;">' + font.traits + '</div>' : ''}
            ${font.notes ? '<div style="font-size:11.5px;color:var(--ff-ink-dim);margin-top:4px;font-style:italic;">' + font.notes + '</div>' : ''}
          </div>
          ${font.reasoning ? '<div class="ff-reason-toggle" data-reason-id="r' + i + '"><span class="arrow">▶</span> Why this font?</div><div class="ff-reasoning" id="r' + i + '">' + font.reasoning + '</div>' : ''}
        `;

        resultsBody.appendChild(card);

        // Animate confidence bar after insertion
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
          const fill = card.querySelector('.ff-conf-fill');
          if (fill) fill.style.width = fill.dataset.width + '%';
        });

        // Collapsible reasoning
        const toggle = card.querySelector('.ff-reason-toggle');
        if (toggle) {
          toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const box = document.getElementById(toggle.dataset.reasonId);
            const open = box.style.display === 'block';
            box.style.display = open ? 'none' : 'block';
            toggle.classList.toggle('open', !open);
          });
        }
      });
    }

    /* ── Loading state with progress steps ── */
    function setLoading(on) {
      if (on) {
        findBtn.disabled = true;
        progressEl.style.display = 'block';
        // Reset steps
        document.querySelectorAll('.ff-step').forEach(s => { s.classList.remove('active','done'); });
        // Clear previous cards (keep progress)
        [...resultsBody.children].forEach(c => {
          if (c !== progressEl) c.remove();
        });
        // Animate steps
        const steps = ['ffStep1','ffStep2','ffStep3','ffStep4'];
        const delays = [0, 700, 1600, 2700];
        steps.forEach((id, i) => {
          setTimeout(() => {
            if (i > 0) document.getElementById(steps[i-1])?.classList.replace('active','done');
            document.getElementById(id)?.classList.add('active');
          }, delays[i]);
        });
      } else {
        document.querySelectorAll('.ff-step').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
        progressEl.style.display = 'none';
        findBtn.disabled = false;
      }
    }

    function resetResults() {
      allFonts = [];
      resultsBody.innerHTML = '';
      resultsBody.appendChild(progressEl);
      progressEl.style.display = 'none';
      filterRow.style.display = 'none';
      resultsLabel.textContent = 'Drop an image to identify fonts';
    }

    function showError(msg) {
      errorEl.textContent = msg;
      errorEl.style.display = 'block';
      resultsLabel.textContent = 'Analysis failed';
    }
  })();
  </script>
</div>

<div class="toast" id="toast"><span class="dot"></span><span id="toastMsg">Exported</span></div>

<script>
/* =========================================================
   API KEYS
   ========================================================= */
// NOTE: no keys are hardcoded here on purpose. Every key used by this app is
// entered by the user in the relevant tab's UI and stored in their own
// browser's localStorage only — it is never bundled into this file or sent
// anywhere except directly to that provider's API. This matters because this
// HTML file can end up hosted/deployed publicly (e.g. on Render): a key typed
// into the source code would be visible to anyone who views the page source.
function getRemoveBgKey() { return 'wYRZM4TRwsDhcJ94uKA6kNna' || localStorage.getItem('bg_apikey_removebg') || ''; }

/* ── Anthropic key — read from the GenMock/FontFinder saved key, never hardcoded ── */
function requireAnthropicKey() {
  return localStorage.getItem('gm_apikey_anthropic') || localStorage.getItem('ais_anthropic_key') || localStorage.getItem('ff_anthropic_key') || '';
}

   ========================================================= */

/* =========================================================
   SCENE RENDERERS — stylised vector "photo" base layers
   ========================================================= */

/* ── Tin Can renderer ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function drawTinCan(ctx, w, h) {
  // Background
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.1,w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0,'#E8E4DB'); bgGrad.addColorStop(1,'#C5BFB0');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  const cx = w*0.5, bodyTop = h*0.14, bodyBot = h*0.86;
  const rx = w*0.22, bodyH = bodyBot - bodyTop;

  // Drop shadow
  ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.18; ctx.filter = 'blur(22px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyBot+24, rx*0.85, 18, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // Cylinder body (gradient for metallic sheen)
  const bodyGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx-rx, 0, cx+rx, 0);
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0,   '#7a8090');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0.12,'#c8cdd8');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0.38,'#e8eaf0');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0.55,'#f5f6fa');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0.72,'#d0d4de');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(0.88,'#9aa0ae');
  bodyGrad.addColorStop(1,   '#6a7080');
  ctx.fillStyle = bodyGrad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx-rx, bodyTop);
  ctx.lineTo(cx-rx, bodyBot);
  ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyBot, rx, rx*0.28, 0, Math.PI, 0);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+rx, bodyTop);
  ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyTop, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI, true);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  // Top ellipse cap (lid)
  ctx.fillStyle = '#c2c8d5';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyTop, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  // Lid highlight rim
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8eaf2'; ctx.lineWidth = 3;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyTop, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  // Bottom rim seam
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.22)'; ctx.lineWidth = 4;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyBot, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  // Top seam line
  const seamY1 = bodyTop + bodyH*0.06;
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'; ctx.lineWidth = 3;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, seamY1, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  // Bottom seam line
  const seamY2 = bodyBot - bodyH*0.06;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, seamY2, rx, rx*0.28, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  // Pull tab on top
  ctx.fillStyle = '#a0a8b8';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx+rx*0.25, bodyTop-rx*0.05, rx*0.22, rx*0.07, -0.25, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#80889a'; ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx+rx*0.25, bodyTop-rx*0.05, rx*0.22, rx*0.07, -0.25, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  return { front: [[cx-rx,bodyTop+bodyH*0.06],[cx+rx,bodyTop+bodyH*0.06],[cx+rx,seamY2],[cx-rx,seamY2]] };
}

function drawTinCanTop(ctx, w, h) {
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.1,w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0,'#E8E4DB'); bgGrad.addColorStop(1,'#C5BFB0');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
  const cx = w*0.5, cy = h*0.45, rx = w*0.26, ry = w*0.26;
  ctx.fillStyle = '#c2c8d5';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, rx, ry, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  const shine = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx-rx*0.2, cy-ry*0.2, rx*0.05, cx, cy, rx);
  shine.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,0.38)'); shine.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)');
  ctx.fillStyle = shine;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, rx, ry, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
}

/* ── Bottle renderer ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function drawBottle(ctx, w, h) {
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.1,w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0,'#DDE6ED'); bgGrad.addColorStop(1,'#B0BEC5');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  const cx = w*0.5;
  // Bottle proportions
  const baseY = h*0.87, neckTopY = h*0.12, shoulderY = h*0.30, neckBotY = h*0.22;
  const bodyRx = w*0.20, neckRx = w*0.06;

  // Drop shadow
  ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.16; ctx.filter = 'blur(20px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, baseY+18, bodyRx*0.9, 16, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // Glass gradient (greenish-clear)
  const glassGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx-bodyRx, 0, cx+bodyRx, 0);
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(80,100,90,0.75)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.12,'rgba(130,165,145,0.80)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.35,'rgba(200,230,210,0.85)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.52,'rgba(230,250,235,0.90)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.70,'rgba(160,200,175,0.82)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.88,'rgba(100,130,115,0.78)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(60,85,75,0.72)');

  // Draw bottle silhouette path
  ctx.beginPath();
  // Base ellipse bottom
  ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyRx, baseY);
  // Left side up to shoulder
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx - bodyRx, shoulderY + h*0.02, cx - neckRx*2.2, shoulderY - h*0.02, cx - neckRx, neckBotY);
  // Neck left
  ctx.lineTo(cx - neckRx, neckTopY + h*0.04);
  // Top cap
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx - neckRx, neckTopY, cx - neckRx*0.6, neckTopY - h*0.01, cx, neckTopY - h*0.01);
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx + neckRx*0.6, neckTopY - h*0.01, cx + neckRx, neckTopY, cx + neckRx, neckTopY + h*0.04);
  // Neck right
  ctx.lineTo(cx + neckRx, neckBotY);
  // Shoulder right side
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx + neckRx*2.2, shoulderY - h*0.02, cx + bodyRx, shoulderY + h*0.02, cx + bodyRx, baseY);
  // Bottom
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = glassGrad;
  ctx.fill();

  // Base ellipse
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, baseY, bodyRx, bodyRx*0.15, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(60,80,70,0.45)'; ctx.fill();

  // Highlight stripe (left)
  const hiGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - bodyRx*0.55, 0, cx - bodyRx*0.25, 0);
  hiGrad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  hiGrad.addColorStop(0.5,'rgba(255,255,255,0.32)');
  hiGrad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  ctx.fillStyle = hiGrad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyRx*0.55, shoulderY);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyRx*0.55, baseY - h*0.02);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyRx*0.25, baseY - h*0.02);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyRx*0.25, shoulderY);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  // Bottle cap/cork
  ctx.fillStyle = '#2d2d30';
  roundRect(ctx, cx - neckRx, neckTopY - h*0.022, neckRx*2, h*0.03, 4);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#4a4a50';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, neckTopY - h*0.022, neckRx, neckRx*0.45, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();

  // Neck ring seam
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.22)'; ctx.lineWidth = 2.5;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx, neckBotY + h*0.01, neckRx, neckRx*0.35, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();

  // Label zone overlay (slight darkening band for design placement)
  const labelTop = shoulderY + h*0.05, labelBot = baseY - h*0.08;
  const labelGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - bodyRx, 0, cx + bodyRx, 0);
  labelGrad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0.10)');
  labelGrad.addColorStop(0.2,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
  labelGrad.addColorStop(0.8,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
  labelGrad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.10)');
  ctx.fillStyle = labelGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(cx - bodyRx, labelTop, bodyRx*2, labelBot - labelTop);

  return { front: [[cx - bodyRx, labelTop],[cx + bodyRx, labelTop],[cx + bodyRx, labelBot],[cx - bodyRx, labelBot]] };
}

function drawBottleTop(ctx, w, h) {
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.05,w*0.5,h*0.5,w*0.6);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0,'#DDE6ED'); bgGrad.addColorStop(1,'#B0BEC5');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
  const cx = w*0.5, cy = h*0.45, r = w*0.10;
  ctx.fillStyle = '#5a7060';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.28)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx - r*0.25, cy - r*0.25, r*0.45, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
}

/* ── Square / Mason-Jar Bottle (coconut oil style) ───────────────────────── */
function drawSquareBottle(ctx, w, h) {
  // ── Background: warm studio bokeh ──
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.45, w*0.05, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.85);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#D6DFCA');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0.55, '#B5C4A6');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(1,  '#8AAA78');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);

  // Soft blurred bokeh blobs
  ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.18; ctx.filter = 'blur(40px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#E8F0D0'; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.18, h*0.3, 90, 90, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#F2EAB8'; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.82, h*0.65, 70, 70, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── Layout constants ──
  const cx   = w * 0.5;
  const bodyW = w * 0.34;          // half-width of the rectangular body
  const bodyTop  = h * 0.185;      // where the shoulder meets the neck base
  const bodyBot  = h * 0.875;      // bottom of bottle
  const bodyH    = bodyBot - bodyTop;

  // Neck geometry (short, centered, slightly narrower)
  const neckHW   = w * 0.072;      // half-width of neck
  const neckTop  = h * 0.075;      // top of neck / bottom of cap
  const neckBot  = bodyTop;        // neck meets shoulders

  // Shoulder — gentle inward taper from body to neck
  const shoulderH = h * 0.05;

  // ── Drop shadow ──
  ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.22; ctx.filter = 'blur(18px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#1a2210';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, bodyBot + 14, bodyW * 0.85, 16, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill(); ctx.restore();

  // ── GLASS BODY: clear with very faint green tint ──
  // Build the full silhouette path (left → up → right → down)
  ctx.save();
  ctx.beginPath();
  // Bottom-left corner (rounded)
  ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyW + 10, bodyBot);
  ctx.arcTo(cx - bodyW, bodyBot, cx - bodyW, bodyBot - 10, 8);
  // Left side straight up
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH);
  // Left shoulder taper to neck
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx - bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH*0.2, cx - neckHW - 8, bodyTop - shoulderH*0.1, cx - neckHW, neckBot);
  // Neck left
  ctx.lineTo(cx - neckHW, neckTop + 4);
  // Neck top-left corner
  ctx.arcTo(cx - neckHW, neckTop, cx - neckHW + 4, neckTop, 4);
  // Neck top
  ctx.lineTo(cx + neckHW - 4, neckTop);
  // Neck top-right corner
  ctx.arcTo(cx + neckHW, neckTop, cx + neckHW, neckTop + 4, 4);
  // Neck right
  ctx.lineTo(cx + neckHW, neckBot);
  // Right shoulder taper
  ctx.bezierCurveTo(cx + neckHW + 8, bodyTop - shoulderH*0.1, cx + bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH*0.2, cx + bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH);
  // Right side down
  ctx.lineTo(cx + bodyW, bodyBot - 10);
  // Bottom-right corner
  ctx.arcTo(cx + bodyW, bodyBot, cx + bodyW - 10, bodyBot, 8);
  // Bottom
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyW + 10, bodyBot);
  ctx.closePath();

  // Clear glass gradient — left rim dark → bright highlight → right rim dark
  const glassGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - bodyW, 0, cx + bodyW, 0);
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0,    'rgba(155,175,140,0.82)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.08, 'rgba(210,230,200,0.88)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.22, 'rgba(240,252,235,0.78)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.35, 'rgba(248,255,244,0.55)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.50, 'rgba(252,255,250,0.38)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.65, 'rgba(248,255,244,0.55)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.80, 'rgba(210,228,200,0.78)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(0.93, 'rgba(175,200,158,0.88)');
  glassGrad.addColorStop(1,    'rgba(130,158,120,0.84)');
  ctx.fillStyle = glassGrad;
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── GLASS EDGE LINES (crisp rim for realism) ──
  ctx.save();
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(90,120,80,0.35)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  // Left edge
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH); ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyW, bodyBot); ctx.stroke();
  // Right edge
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx + bodyW, bodyTop + shoulderH); ctx.lineTo(cx + bodyW, bodyBot); ctx.stroke();
  // Bottom
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyW + 8, bodyBot); ctx.lineTo(cx + bodyW - 8, bodyBot); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── BRIGHT LEFT HIGHLIGHT STRIPE ──
  ctx.save();
  const hiX1 = cx - bodyW + bodyW * 0.06;
  const hiX2 = cx - bodyW + bodyW * 0.20;
  const hiGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(hiX1, 0, hiX2, 0);
  hiGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  hiGrad.addColorStop(0.4, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.55)');
  hiGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  ctx.fillStyle = hiGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(hiX1, bodyTop, hiX2 - hiX1, bodyH * 0.85);
  ctx.restore();

  // ── OIL FILL inside the body (golden yellow, semi-transparent) ──
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.38;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx - bodyW + 3, bodyTop + shoulderH);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - bodyW + 3, bodyBot - 3);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + bodyW - 3, bodyBot - 3);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + bodyW - 3, bodyTop + shoulderH);
  ctx.closePath();
  const oilGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - bodyW, 0, cx + bodyW, 0);
  oilGrad.addColorStop(0,   '#c8a630');
  oilGrad.addColorStop(0.5, '#f0d060');
  oilGrad.addColorStop(1,   '#c8a630');
  ctx.fillStyle = oilGrad;
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── LABEL ZONE (where design goes — white-ish rect slightly inside body) ──
  const labelTop  = bodyTop + bodyH * 0.04;
  const labelBot  = bodyBot - bodyH * 0.08;
  const labelPad  = bodyW * 0.06;
  const labelLeft = cx - bodyW + labelPad;
  const labelW    = (bodyW - labelPad) * 2;

  // Subtle label background (slightly lighter than glass)
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.08;
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
  ctx.fillRect(labelLeft, labelTop, labelW, labelBot - labelTop);
  ctx.restore();

  // ── NECK GLASS DETAIL ──
  ctx.save();
  const neckGlassGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - neckHW, 0, cx + neckHW, 0);
  neckGlassGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(155,175,140,0.82)');
  neckGlassGrad.addColorStop(0.25, 'rgba(230,248,225,0.70)');
  neckGlassGrad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(248,255,244,0.50)');
  neckGlassGrad.addColorStop(0.75, 'rgba(230,248,225,0.70)');
  neckGlassGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(155,175,140,0.82)');
  ctx.fillStyle = neckGlassGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(cx - neckHW, neckTop, neckHW * 2, neckBot - neckTop);
  // Neck edge lines
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(80,110,70,0.30)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  ctx.strokeRect(cx - neckHW, neckTop, neckHW * 2, neckBot - neckTop);
  ctx.restore();

  // ── NECK RING / THREAD DETAIL ──
  ctx.save();
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(100,130,90,0.45)'; ctx.lineWidth = 2.5;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - neckHW, neckBot - 8); ctx.lineTo(cx + neckHW, neckBot - 8); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - neckHW, neckBot - 16); ctx.lineTo(cx + neckHW, neckBot - 16); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── GOLD LID / CAP ──
  const capH    = neckTop - h * 0.01;
  const capTop  = h * 0.028;
  const capHW   = neckHW + 4;       // cap slightly wider than neck

  ctx.save();
  // Gold gradient
  const capGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - capHW, 0, cx + capHW, 0);
  capGrad.addColorStop(0,    '#7a5e18');
  capGrad.addColorStop(0.12, '#c49a28');
  capGrad.addColorStop(0.30, '#e8c84a');
  capGrad.addColorStop(0.50, '#f5d85a');
  capGrad.addColorStop(0.68, '#e0bc3a');
  capGrad.addColorStop(0.86, '#b88a20');
  capGrad.addColorStop(1,    '#7a5e18');
  ctx.fillStyle = capGrad;
  roundRect(ctx, cx - capHW, capTop, capHW * 2, capH - capTop, 4);
  ctx.fill();
  // Cap top shine
  const capShine = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - capHW, capTop, cx + capHW, capTop);
  capShine.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  capShine.addColorStop(0.4, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.32)');
  capShine.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(255,255,255,0)');
  ctx.fillStyle = capShine;
  ctx.fillRect(cx - capHW, capTop, capHW * 2, (capH - capTop) * 0.4);
  // Cap ribbed lines
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let ry = capTop + 4; ry < capH - 2; ry += 5) {
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - capHW + 2, ry); ctx.lineTo(cx + capHW - 2, ry); ctx.stroke();
  }
  // Cap bottom edge
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(cx - capHW, capH); ctx.lineTo(cx + capHW, capH); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();

  // ── BOTTOM BASE TINT ──
  const baseGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, bodyBot - 20, 0, bodyBot);
  baseGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
  baseGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)');
  ctx.fillStyle = baseGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(cx - bodyW, bodyBot - 20, bodyW * 2, 20);

  return {
    front: [
      [labelLeft,  labelTop],
      [labelLeft + labelW, labelTop],
      [labelLeft + labelW, labelBot],
      [labelLeft,  labelBot]
    ]
  };
}

function drawSquareBottleTop(ctx, w, h) {
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.45, w*0.05, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.65);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#D6DFCA'); bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#8AAA78');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad; ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);

  const cx = w*0.5, cy = h*0.48;
  const capHW = w*0.085, capH = w*0.088;
  // Gold cap top view
  const capGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - capHW, cy - capH, cx + capHW, cy + capH);
  capGrad.addColorStop(0, '#7a5e18'); capGrad.addColorStop(0.4, '#f5d85a'); capGrad.addColorStop(1, '#7a5e18');
  ctx.fillStyle = capGrad;
  roundRect(ctx, cx - capHW, cy - capH, capHW*2, capH*2, 4);
  ctx.fill();
  // Shine
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(cx - capHW*0.3, cy - capH*0.3, capHW*0.5, capH*0.3, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
}

function bgWash(ctx,w,h,c1,c2){
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h);
  g.addColorStop(0,c1); g.addColorStop(1,c2);
  ctx.fillStyle = g;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
}

function drawTshirt(ctx,w,h, shirtColor='#fbfaf7', shadowColor='#000000'){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#e9e6df','#cfcabd');
  ctx.save();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.92,260,40,0,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = shirtColor;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.30,h*0.18);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.16,h*0.27);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.23,h*0.40);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.27,h*0.36);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.25,h*0.92);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.5,h*0.97,w*0.75,h*0.92);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.73,h*0.36);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.77,h*0.40);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.84,h*0.27);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.70,h*0.18);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.5,h*0.27,w*0.30,h*0.18);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.185,55,18,0,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = shadeColor(shirtColor,-10);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.07)';
  ctx.lineWidth=10;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.36,h*0.40); ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.40,h*0.6,w*0.37,h*0.85);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.64,h*0.40); ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.60,h*0.6,w*0.63,h*0.85);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
}

function shadeColor(hex, percent){
  const n = parseInt(hex.replace('#',''),16);
  let r=(n>>16)+percent, g=(n>>8&0x00FF)+percent, b=(n&0x0000FF)+percent;
  r=Math.max(Math.min(255,r),0); g=Math.max(Math.min(255,g),0); b=Math.max(Math.min(255,b),0);
  return '#'+(0x1000000+r*0x10000+g*0x100+b).toString(16).slice(1);
}

function drawPoster(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#d8d3c6','#b9b2a0');
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.03)';
  for(let i=0;i<40;i++){
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(Math.random()*w,Math.random()*h);
    ctx.lineTo(Math.random()*w,Math.random()*h);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.265,h*0.12,420,700);
  ctx.fillStyle='#3a342c';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.25,h*0.10,420,700);
  ctx.fillStyle='#efece5';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.25+18,h*0.10+18,420-36,700-36);
}

function drawPhone(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#cfd6da','#9aa6ad');
  ctx.fillStyle='#caa583';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.18,h);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.15,h*0.55,w*0.30,h*0.42);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.5,h*0.30,w*0.75,h*0.40);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.92,h*0.55,w*0.88,h);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.25)';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.315,h*0.13,322,720);
  const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(w*0.3,0,w*0.7,0);
  grad.addColorStop(0,'#2b2c2f'); grad.addColorStop(1,'#1a1b1d');
  ctx.fillStyle = grad;
  roundRect(ctx,w*0.31,h*0.12,320,720,40); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#0a0a0b';
  roundRect(ctx,w*0.31+10,h*0.12+10,300,700,30); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#1a1b1d';
  roundRect(ctx,w*0.5-40,h*0.12+18,80,18,9); ctx.fill();
}

function drawCard(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#7d6a52','#5b4c3a');
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
  for(let i=0;i<14;i++){
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(0,i*90+Math.sin(i)*10);
    ctx.bezierCurveTo(w*0.3,i*90+20,w*0.7,i*90-20,w,i*90+Math.sin(i)*10);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(8,10);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.25)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.20,h*0.39); ctx.lineTo(w*0.845,h*0.355);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.86,h*0.59); ctx.lineTo(w*0.215,h*0.625);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();
  ctx.fillStyle='#f7f5f0';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.20,h*0.39); ctx.lineTo(w*0.845,h*0.355);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.86,h*0.59); ctx.lineTo(w*0.215,h*0.625);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
}

  ctx.fillStyle='#e9e6df';
  ctx.beginPath();

  ctx.lineTo(w*0.89,h*0.43); ctx.lineTo(w*0.11,h*0.47);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
}

function drawTote(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#ddd6c4','#bfb6a0');
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.1)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.92,220,30,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#e4ddc9';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.28,h*0.34);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.72,h*0.34);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.78,h*0.90);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.22,h*0.90);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(w*0.38,h*0.34); ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.38,h*0.18,w*0.46,h*0.18); ctx.stroke();
