  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.06)'; ctx.lineWidth=20;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(w*0.5,h*0.34); ctx.lineTo(w*0.5,h*0.90); ctx.stroke();
}

function drawMug(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#cdd2cf','#a3aba6');
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.93,190,26,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#f4f1ea';
  roundRect(ctx,w*0.28,h*0.36,330,330,16); ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle='#f4f1ea'; ctx.lineWidth=34; ctx.lineCap='round';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(w*0.28+330+10,h*0.36+165,80,Math.PI*0.7,Math.PI*1.4);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.28,h*0.36,330,14);
}

function draw3DTexture(ctx, quad, opacity) {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...quad[0]);
  ctx.lineTo(...quad[1]);
  ctx.lineTo(...quad[2]);
  ctx.lineTo(...quad[3]);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.clip();

  const xs = quad.map(p => p[0]);
  const ys = quad.map(p => p[1]);
  const minX = Math.min(...xs), maxX = Math.max(...xs);
  const minY = Math.min(...ys), maxY = Math.max(...ys);
  const w = maxX - minX, h = maxY - minY;

  ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(0,0,0,${0.035 * (opacity || 1)})`;
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = 4; i < w; i += 6) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(minX + i, minY);
    ctx.lineTo(minX + i, maxY);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(0,0,0,${0.035 * (opacity || 1)})`;
  let seed = 42;
  function random() {
    let x = Math.sin(seed++) * 10000;
    return x - Math.floor(x);
  }
  for (let i = 0; i < 40; i++) {
    const rx = minX + random() * w;
    const ry = minY + random() * h;
    if (isPointInQuad([rx, ry], quad)) {
      ctx.fillRect(rx, ry, random() * 2 + 1, random() * 2 + 1);
    }
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function isPointInQuad(p, quad) {
  let inside = false;
  for (let i = 0, j = quad.length - 1; i < quad.length; j = i++) {
    const xi = quad[i][0], yi = quad[i][1];
    const xj = quad[j][0], yj = quad[j][1];
    const intersect = ((yi > p[1]) !== (yj > p[1]))
        && (p[0] < (xj - xi) * (p[1] - yi) / (yj - yi) + xi);
    if (intersect) inside = !inside;
  }
  return inside;
}

/* =========================================================
   ENHANCED 3D BOX RENDERER
   Draws a realistic 3D isometric box with the user's design
   texture-mapped onto front, side, and top faces.
   ========================================================= */

function drawBox(ctx,w,h, opts){
  opts = opts || {};
  const square = !!opts.square;
  const tube = !!opts.tube;

  // Neutral studio background with subtle vignette
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.15, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#EBE8E0');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0.6, '#E0DCD2');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#C8C2B4');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  // Soft floor plane gradient
  const floorY = h * 0.72;
  const floorGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, floorY, 0, h);
  floorGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
  floorGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)');
  ctx.fillStyle = floorGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(0, floorY, w, h - floorY);

  // === 3D BOX GEOMETRY ===
  // Front face (the primary design face)
  // Tube box: long slim carton — wide length, moderate height, shallow depth.
  const frontW = tube ? w*0.58 : (square ? w*0.42 : w*0.41);
  const frontH = tube ? h*0.26 : (square ? w*0.42 : w*0.38);
  const depthX = tube ? w*0.085 : w*0.10;
  const depthY = tube ? h*0.115 : h*0.08;

  // Position the box centrally
  const boxCX = tube ? w*0.44 : w*0.46;
  const boxCY = tube ? h*0.545 : h*0.52;

  const fTL = [boxCX - frontW/2, boxCY - frontH/2 + depthY/2];
  const fTR = [boxCX + frontW/2, boxCY - frontH/2 + depthY/2];
  const fBR = [boxCX + frontW/2, boxCY + frontH/2 + depthY/2];
  const fBL = [boxCX - frontW/2, boxCY + frontH/2 + depthY/2];

  // Side face (right face, visible in 3/4 view)
  const sideW = tube ? w*0.085 : (square ? w*0.10 : w*0.08);
  const sTL = [fTR[0], fTR[1]];
  const sTR = [fTR[0] + depthX, fTR[1] - depthY];
  const sBR = [fBR[0] + depthX, fBR[1] - depthY];
  const sBL = [fBR[0], fBR[1]];

  // Top face
  const tBL = [fTL[0], fTL[1]];
  const tBR = [fTR[0], fTR[1]];
  const tTR = [fTR[0] + depthX, fTR[1] - depthY];
  const tTL = [fTL[0] + depthX, fTL[1] - depthY];

  const frontQuad = [fTL, fTR, fBR, fBL];
  const sideQuad = [sTL, sTR, sBR, sBL];
  const topQuad = [tBL, tBR, tTR, tTL];

  // === SHADOWS ===
  // Large diffuse shadow behind box
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.15;
  ctx.filter = 'blur(25px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(fBL[0]+15, fBL[1]+10);
  ctx.lineTo(sBR[0]+20, sBR[1]+10);
  ctx.lineTo(sBR[0]+25, sBR[1]+25);
  ctx.lineTo(fBL[0]+10, fBL[1]+25);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // Floor contact shadow
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.3;
  ctx.filter = 'blur(6px)';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(fBL[0]+3, fBL[1]+2);
  ctx.lineTo(sBR[0]+5, sBR[1]+2);
  ctx.lineTo(sBR[0]+5, sBR[1]+8);
  ctx.lineTo(fBL[0]+3, fBL[1]+8);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  // === DRAW FACES (back-to-front painter's order) ===

  // Side face - slightly darker tint
  ctx.fillStyle='#B8AD95';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...sTL); ctx.lineTo(...sTR); ctx.lineTo(...sBR); ctx.lineTo(...sBL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  // Side face lighting gradient (darker towards right = away from light)
  const sideGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(sTL[0], 0, sTR[0], 0);
  sideGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)');
  sideGrad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)');
  sideGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)');
  ctx.fillStyle = sideGrad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...sTL); ctx.lineTo(...sTR); ctx.lineTo(...sBR); ctx.lineTo(...sBL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  draw3DTexture(ctx, sideQuad, 0.6);

  // Top face - lighter
  ctx.fillStyle='#EDE9DD';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...tBL); ctx.lineTo(...tBR); ctx.lineTo(...tTR); ctx.lineTo(...tTL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  // Top face subtle gradient
  const topGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, tTL[1], 0, tBL[1]);
  topGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)');
  topGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)');
  ctx.fillStyle = topGrad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...tBL); ctx.lineTo(...tBR); ctx.lineTo(...tTR); ctx.lineTo(...tTL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  draw3DTexture(ctx, topQuad, 0.4);

  // Front face - mid tone (design goes here)
  ctx.fillStyle='#DCD5C2';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...fTL); ctx.lineTo(...fTR); ctx.lineTo(...fBR); ctx.lineTo(...fBL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  // Subtle front face lighting
  const frontGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(fTL[0], 0, fTR[0], 0);
  frontGrad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)');
  frontGrad.addColorStop(0.6, 'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
  frontGrad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)');
  ctx.fillStyle = frontGrad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(...fTL); ctx.lineTo(...fTR); ctx.lineTo(...fBR); ctx.lineTo(...fBL);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

  draw3DTexture(ctx, frontQuad, 0.5);

  // === CRISP EDGES ===
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.22)';
  ctx.lineWidth=1.5;
  // Front face outline
  [[fTL,fTR],[fTR,fBR],[fBR,fBL],[fBL,fTL]].forEach(([a,b])=>{
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...a); ctx.lineTo(...b); ctx.stroke();
  });
  // Side edges
  [[sTL,sTR],[sTR,sBR],[sBR,sBL]].forEach(([a,b])=>{
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...a); ctx.lineTo(...b); ctx.stroke();
  });
  // Top edges
  [[tBL,tTL],[tTL,tTR]].forEach(([a,b])=>{
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...a); ctx.lineTo(...b); ctx.stroke();
  });

  // Highlight on top-left front edge (light source from upper-left)
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';
  ctx.lineWidth=1;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...fTL); ctx.lineTo(...fBL); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...tBL); ctx.lineTo(...tTL); ctx.stroke();

  return {
    front: frontQuad,
    side: sideQuad,
    top: topQuad
  };
}

function drawPaperTexture(ctx, x, y, w, h) {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.035)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = 4; i < w; i += 6) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x + i, y + 2);
    ctx.lineTo(x + i, y + h - 2);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.035)';
  for (let i = 0; i < 40; i++) {
    const rx = x + 5 + Math.random() * (w - 10);
    const ry = y + 5 + Math.random() * (h - 10);
    ctx.fillRect(rx, ry, Math.random() * 2 + 1, Math.random() * 2 + 1);
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawBeveledPanel(ctx, x, y, w, h, baseColor) {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.fillStyle = baseColor;
  ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
  drawPaperTexture(ctx, x, y, w, h);

  const thickness = 5;
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.fillRect(x, y + h - thickness, w, thickness);
  ctx.fillRect(x + w - thickness, y, thickness, h);
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.22)';
  ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, thickness);
  ctx.fillRect(x, y, thickness, h);

  const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(x, y, x + w, y + h);
  grad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)');
  grad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)');
  ctx.fillStyle = grad;
  ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, h);

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.22)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  ctx.strokeRect(x, y, w, h);
  
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawBoxFront(ctx, w, h, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  const square = !!opts.square;
  const tube = !!opts.tube;

  // Studio background
  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.15, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#EBE8E0');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0.6, '#E0DCD2');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#C8C2B4');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  const fw = tube ? 560 : 370;
  const fh = tube ? 270 : (square ? 370 : 340);
  const cx = w*0.5;
  const bx = cx - fw/2;
  const by = tube ? 400 : (square ? 330 : 380);

  // Shadow
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh, fw*0.52, 14, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh, fw*0.48, 4, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  drawBeveledPanel(ctx, bx, by, fw, fh, '#dcd5c2');

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  
  const flapH = tube ? 40 : (square ? 60 : 50);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(bx + 4, by + flapH);
  ctx.lineTo(bx + fw - 4, by + flapH);
  ctx.moveTo(bx + 4, by + fh - flapH);
  ctx.lineTo(bx + fw - 4, by + fh - flapH);
  ctx.stroke();
}

function drawBoxSide(ctx, w, h, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  const square = !!opts.square;
  const tube = !!opts.tube;

  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.15, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#EBE8E0');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0.6, '#E0DCD2');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#C8C2B4');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  const fw = tube ? 80 : (square ? 370 : 180);
  const fh = tube ? 270 : (square ? 370 : 340);
  const cx = w*0.5;
  const bx = cx - fw/2;
  const by = tube ? 400 : (square ? 330 : 380);

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh, fw*0.52, 14, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh, fw*0.48, 4, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  drawBeveledPanel(ctx, bx, by, fw, fh, '#a89c82');

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  const flapH = tube ? 40 : (square ? 70 : 60);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(bx + 4, by + flapH);
  ctx.lineTo(bx + fw - 4, by + flapH);
  ctx.moveTo(bx + 4, by + fh - flapH);
  ctx.lineTo(bx + fw - 4, by + fh - flapH);
  ctx.stroke();

  if (!tube) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(bx + fw/2, by + flapH);
    ctx.lineTo(bx + fw/2, by + fh - flapH);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
}

function drawBoxTop(ctx, w, h, opts) {
  opts = opts || {};
  const square = !!opts.square;
  const tube = !!opts.tube;

  const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.15, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.7);
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#EBE8E0');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(0.6, '#E0DCD2');
  bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#C8C2B4');
  ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

  const fw = tube ? 560 : 370;
  const fh = tube ? 120 : (square ? 370 : 180);
  const cx = w*0.5;
  const bx = cx - fw/2;
  const by = tube ? 270 : (square ? 330 : 460);

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh/2 + 4, fw/2 + 15, fh/2 + 12, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();
  
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.22)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by + fh/2, fw/2 + 5, fh/2 + 3, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  drawBeveledPanel(ctx, bx, by, fw, fh, '#f0ece1');

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  if (square) {
    ctx.moveTo(bx + fw/2, by + 4);
    ctx.lineTo(bx + fw/2, by + fh - 4);
  } else {
    ctx.moveTo(bx + 4, by + fh/2);
    ctx.lineTo(bx + fw - 4, by + fh/2);
  }
  ctx.stroke();

  const tapeColor = 'rgba(200,165,120,0.48)';
  ctx.fillStyle = tapeColor;
  ctx.save();
  
  if (square) {
    const tx = bx + fw/2 - 20, ty = by - 5, tw = 40, th = fh + 10;
    ctx.fillRect(tx, ty, tw, th);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(120,95,70,0.15)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.strokeRect(tx, ty, tw, th);
    
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(tx + 6, ty + 10); ctx.lineTo(tx + 18, ty + 40);
    ctx.moveTo(tx + 22, ty + h*0.3); ctx.lineTo(tx + 34, ty + h*0.3 + 30);
    ctx.stroke();
  } else {
    const tx = bx - 5, ty = by + fh/2 - (tube ? 12 : 20), tw = fw + 10, th = tube ? 24 : 40;
    ctx.fillRect(tx, ty, tw, th);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(120,95,70,0.15)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.strokeRect(tx, ty, tw, th);
    
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(tx + 20, ty + 6); ctx.lineTo(tx + 50, ty + 18);
    ctx.moveTo(tx + w*0.4, ty + 22); ctx.lineTo(tx + w*0.4 + 30, ty + 34);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawSachetSide(ctx, w, h) {
  bgWash(ctx, w, h, '#e6e1d4', '#c9c1ab');

  const cx = w*0.5;
  const txL = cx - 15, txR = cx + 15, ty = 300;
  const bxR = cx + 60, bxL = cx - 60, by = 760;

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by, 75, 12, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, by, 62, 4, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = '#f2efe6';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(txL, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(txR, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(bxR, by);
  ctx.lineTo(bxL, by);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)';
  ctx.fillRect(txL, ty, 30, 30);
  
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = ty + 3; i < ty + 30; i += 4) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(txL, i);
    ctx.lineTo(txR, i);
    ctx.stroke();
  }

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(bxL, by - 12);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cx, by - 2, bxR, by - 12);
  ctx.stroke();

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx, ty + 30);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, by - 8);
  ctx.stroke();

  const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(bxL, 0, bxR, 0);
  grad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.14)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.2, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.22)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.8, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)');
  grad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)');
  
  ctx.fillStyle = grad;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(txL, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(txR, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(bxR, by);
  ctx.lineTo(bxL, by);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(txL, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(txR, ty);
  ctx.lineTo(bxR, by);
  ctx.lineTo(bxL, by);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.stroke();
}

function drawSachetTop(ctx, w, h) {
  bgWash(ctx, w, h, '#e6e1d4', '#c9c1ab');

  const cx = w*0.5;
  const cy = 550;
  
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, cy + 12, 140, 60, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();
  
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.16)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, cy + 5, 125, 52, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle = '#f2efe6';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, 120, 50, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.save();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, 114, 45, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.clip();
  
  ctx.fillStyle = '#dcdde1';
  ctx.fillRect(cx - 120, cy - 50, 240, 100);
  
  const foilGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(cx - 114, 0, cx + 114, 0);
  foilGrad.addColorStop(0, '#c8cbcd');
  foilGrad.addColorStop(0.25, '#f5f6f8');
  foilGrad.addColorStop(0.45, '#a5a9ac');
  foilGrad.addColorStop(0.55, '#a5a9ac');
  foilGrad.addColorStop(0.75, '#f5f6f8');
  foilGrad.addColorStop(1, '#c8cbcd');
  ctx.fillStyle = foilGrad;
  ctx.fillRect(cx - 120, cy - 50, 240, 100);
  ctx.restore();

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.22)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 3.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx - 120, cy);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + 120, cy);
  ctx.stroke();

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx - 120, cy - 4);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + 120, cy - 4);
  ctx.moveTo(cx - 120, cy + 4);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + 120, cy + 4);
  ctx.stroke();

  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 2.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx, cy, 120, 50, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.stroke();
}

function drawSachet(ctx,w,h){
  bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#e6e1d4','#c9c1ab');

  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.13)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.94,170,26,0,0,Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.save();
  ctx.fillStyle='#f2efe6';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.645,h*0.255);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.675,h*0.40,w*0.655,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.645,h*0.78,w*0.60,h*0.86);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.40,h*0.86);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.355,h*0.78,w*0.345,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.325,h*0.40,w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
  ctx.fillRect(w*0.34,h*0.24,w*0.32,h*0.025);

  ctx.fillStyle; // keep
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.355,h*0.262); ctx.lineTo(w*0.375,h*0.262); ctx.lineTo(w*0.365,h*0.28);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle='#cdc6b2';
  ctx.fill();

  const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(w*0.32,0,w*0.68,0);
  grad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0.10)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.18,'rgba(255,255,255,0.10)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.5,'rgba(255,255,255,0.22)');
  grad.addColorStop(0.82,'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)');
  grad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0.14)');
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.645,h*0.255);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.675,h*0.40,w*0.655,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.645,h*0.78,w*0.60,h*0.86);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.40,h*0.86);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.355,h*0.78,w*0.345,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.325,h*0.40,w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = grad;
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.12)';
  ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.40,h*0.835); ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.5,h*0.86,w*0.60,h*0.835);
  ctx.stroke();

  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.16)';
  ctx.lineWidth=2;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.645,h*0.255);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.675,h*0.40,w*0.655,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.645,h*0.78,w*0.60,h*0.86);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.40,h*0.86);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.355,h*0.78,w*0.345,h*0.62);
  ctx.quadraticCurveTo(w*0.325,h*0.40,w*0.355,h*0.255);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
}

function roundRect(ctx,x,y,w,h,r){
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(x+r,y);
  ctx.arcTo(x+w,y,x+w,y+h,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x+w,y+h,x,y+h,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x,y+h,x,y,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x,y,x+w,y,r);
  ctx.closePath();
}

/* =========================================================
   360° TURNTABLE RIGS
   ========================================================= */

function turntableFrame(tpl, angleDeg){
  const a = ((angleDeg % 360) + 360) % 360;
  const rad = a * Math.PI/180;
  if(tpl.rig === 'box') return boxTurntableFrame(tpl, a, rad);
  if(tpl.rig === 'sachet') return sachetTurntableFrame(tpl, a, rad);
  return null;
}

function facing(rad){ return Math.cos(rad); }

function boxTurntableFrame(tpl, a, rad){
  const square = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.square);
  const tube = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.tube);
  const f = facing(rad);
  const visibleFront = f > -0.02;
  const widthScale = Math.max(Math.abs(f), 0.045);

  const draw = (ctx,w,h)=>{
    // Studio background
    const bgGrad = ctx.createRadialGradient(w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.15, w*0.5, h*0.5, w*0.7);
    bgGrad.addColorStop(0, '#EBE8E0');
    bgGrad.addColorStop(0.6, '#E0DCD2');
    bgGrad.addColorStop(1, '#C8C2B4');
    ctx.fillStyle = bgGrad;
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.14)';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.92,260,30,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();

    const baseTop    = tube ? [w*0.16,h*0.375] : (square ? [w*0.26,h*0.30] : [w*0.29,h*0.27]);
    const baseTopR   = tube ? [w*0.79,h*0.375] : (square ? [w*0.6722,h*0.30] : [w*0.70,h*0.27]);
    const baseBotR   = tube ? [w*0.79,h*0.620] : (square ? [w*0.6722,h*0.636] : [w*0.70,h*0.582]);
    const baseBotL   = tube ? [w*0.16,h*0.620] : (square ? [w*0.26,h*0.636] : [w*0.29,h*0.582]);
    const cx0 = (baseTop[0]+baseTopR[0])/2;

    const squeeze = (p)=> [ cx0 + (p[0]-cx0)*widthScale, p[1] ];
    const frontTop = squeeze(baseTop), frontTopR = squeeze(baseTopR);
    const frontBotR = squeeze(baseBotR), frontBotL = squeeze(baseBotL);

    const depthFull = tube ? w*0.075 : w*0.09, depthYFull = tube ? h*0.10 : h*0.075;
    const sideDir = f >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
    const depthX = sideDir * depthFull * (1 - Math.abs(f)*0.55);
    const depthY = depthYFull * (1 - Math.abs(f)*0.35);

        const sideAnchorT = sideDir>0 ? frontTopR : frontTop;
    const sideAnchorB = sideDir>0 ? frontBotR : frontBotL;
    const topBackL  = [ (sideDir>0?frontTop:frontTopR)[0] + depthX, (sideDir>0?frontTop:frontTopR)[1]-depthY ];
    const topBackR  = [ sideAnchorT[0] + depthX, sideAnchorT[1]-depthY ];
    const sideBackR = [ sideAnchorB[0] + depthX, sideAnchorB[1]-depthY ];

    const tFL = frontTop;
    const tFR = frontTopR;
    const tBL = sideDir > 0 ? topBackL : topBackR;
    const tBR = sideDir > 0 ? topBackR : topBackL;

    const sideQuad = [sideAnchorT, topBackR, sideBackR, sideAnchorB];
    const topQuad = [tFL, tFR, tBR, tBL];
    const frontQuad = [frontTop, frontTopR, frontBotR, frontBotL];

    // side face
    ctx.fillStyle='#B8AD95';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...sideAnchorT); ctx.lineTo(...topBackR); ctx.lineTo(...sideBackR); ctx.lineTo(...sideAnchorB);
    ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
    draw3DTexture(ctx, sideQuad, 1.2);

    // top face
    ctx.fillStyle='#EDE9DD';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...topQuad[0]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[1]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[2]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[3]);
    ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
    draw3DTexture(ctx, topQuad, 0.8);

    // front face
    ctx.fillStyle='#dcd5c2';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...frontTop); ctx.lineTo(...frontTopR); ctx.lineTo(...frontBotR); ctx.lineTo(...frontBotL);
    ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
    draw3DTexture(ctx, frontQuad, 1.0);

    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.18)'; ctx.lineWidth=2;
        [[frontTop,frontTopR],[frontTopR,frontBotR],[frontBotR,frontBotL],[frontBotL,frontTop],
     [sideAnchorT,topBackR],[topBackR,sideBackR],[sideBackR,sideAnchorB],
     [tFL,tBL],[tFR,tBR],[tBL,tBR]].forEach(([p,q])=>{
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(...p); ctx.lineTo(...q); ctx.stroke();
    });

    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.15)';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...topQuad[0]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[1]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[2]); ctx.lineTo(...topQuad[3]);
    ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();

    const FACE_NAMES = ['front', 'side', 'back', 'other_side'];
    const fIdx = Math.floor((a + 45) / 90) % 4;
    const frontPanelName = FACE_NAMES[fIdx];
    const sidePanelName = FACE_NAMES[sideDir === 1 ? (fIdx + 1) % 4 : (fIdx + 3) % 4];

    return {
      [frontPanelName]: frontQuad,
      [sidePanelName]: sideQuad,
      top: topQuad
    };
  };

  const baseTop    = tube ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.16,tpl.canvas[1]*0.448] : (square ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.26,tpl.canvas[1]*0.30] : [tpl.canvas[0]*0.29,tpl.canvas[1]*0.27]);
  const baseTopR   = tube ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.78,tpl.canvas[1]*0.448] : (square ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.6722,tpl.canvas[1]*0.30] : [tpl.canvas[0]*0.70,tpl.canvas[1]*0.27]);
  const baseBotR   = tube ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.78,tpl.canvas[1]*0.572] : (square ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.6722,tpl.canvas[1]*0.636] : [tpl.canvas[0]*0.70,tpl.canvas[1]*0.582]);
  const baseBotL   = tube ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.16,tpl.canvas[1]*0.572] : (square ? [tpl.canvas[0]*0.26,tpl.canvas[1]*0.636] : [tpl.canvas[0]*0.29,tpl.canvas[1]*0.582]);
  const cx0 = (baseTop[0]+baseTopR[0])/2;
  const squeezeC = (p)=> [ cx0 + (p[0]-cx0)*widthScale, p[1] ];

  return {
    draw,
    corners: [squeezeC(baseTop), squeezeC(baseTopR), squeezeC(baseBotR), squeezeC(baseBotL)],
    designVisible: visibleFront
  };
}

function sachetTurntableFrame(tpl, a, rad){
  const f = facing(rad);
  const widthScale = Math.max(Math.abs(f), 0.05);
  const visibleFront = f > -0.02;

  const baseTL = [tpl.canvas[0]*0.355, tpl.canvas[1]*0.255];
  const baseTR = [tpl.canvas[0]*0.645, tpl.canvas[1]*0.255];
  const baseBR = [tpl.canvas[0]*0.655, tpl.canvas[1]*0.62];
  const baseBL = [tpl.canvas[0]*0.345, tpl.canvas[1]*0.62];
  const cx0 = (baseTL[0]+baseTR[0])/2;
  const squeeze = (p)=> [ cx0 + (p[0]-cx0)*widthScale, p[1] ];

  const draw = (ctx,w,h)=>{
    bgWash(ctx,w,h,'#e6e1d4','#c9c1ab');
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.13)';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*0.5,h*0.94,170,26,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();

    const cx = w*0.5;
    const sx = (x)=> cx + (x-cx)*widthScale;

    ctx.save();
    ctx.fillStyle='#f2efe6';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.255);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.675),h*0.40,sx(w*0.655),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.78,sx(w*0.60),h*0.86);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.40),h*0.86);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.345),h*0.78,sx(w*0.345),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.325),h*0.40,sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fill();

    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
    ctx.fillRect(sx(w*0.34),h*0.24,(sx(w*0.66)-sx(w*0.34)),h*0.025);

    const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(sx(w*0.32),0,sx(w*0.68),0);
    const edge = 1-Math.abs(f);
    grad.addColorStop(0,`rgba(0,0,0,${0.10+edge*0.12})`);
    grad.addColorStop(0.18,'rgba(255,255,255,0.10)');
    grad.addColorStop(0.5,'rgba(255,255,255,0.22)');
    grad.addColorStop(0.82,'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)');
    grad.addColorStop(1,`rgba(0,0,0,${0.14+edge*0.12})`);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.255);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.675),h*0.40,sx(w*0.655),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.78,sx(w*0.60),h*0.86);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.40),h*0.86);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.345),h*0.78,sx(w*0.345),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.325),h*0.40,sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.fill();

    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.16)'; ctx.lineWidth=2;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.255);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.675),h*0.40,sx(w*0.655),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.645),h*0.78,sx(w*0.60),h*0.86);
    ctx.lineTo(sx(w*0.40),h*0.86);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.345),h*0.78,sx(w*0.345),h*0.62);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(sx(w*0.325),h*0.40,sx(w*0.355),h*0.255);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();
  };

  return {
    draw,
    corners: [squeeze(baseTL), squeeze(baseTR), squeeze(baseBR), squeeze(baseBL)],
    designVisible: visibleFront
  };
}

/* =========================================================
   STATE
   ========================================================= */
const state = {
  template: TEMPLATES[0],
  corners: TEMPLATES[0].corners.map(p=>p.slice()),
  designImg: null,
  designName: '',
  blend: TEMPLATES[0].blend,
  opacity: TEMPLATES[0].opacity,
  fit: 'cover',
  pinsVisible: false,
  dragIdx: -1,
  view: '3d',
  customCorners: {},
  lastActivePanel: 'main',
  dielineMode: true,
  perFaceMode: false,
  perFaceImgs: { front: null, side: null, back: null, other_side: null, top: null },
  ttAngle: 0,
  ttPlaying: false,
  ttRafId: null,
  ttLastTs: null,
  customDimsCm: {}   // keyed by template id → { W, H, D } in cm
};

const tplGrid = document.getElementById('tplGrid');

const dropzone = document.getElementById('dropzone');

/* =========================================================
   TEMPLATE THUMBNAILS — tiny rendered previews
   ========================================================= */
function buildTemplateThumb(tpl){
  const c = document.createElement('canvas');
  c.width = 160; c.height = 160;
  const cx = c.getContext('2d');
  cx.save();
  cx.scale(160/tpl.canvas[0], 160/tpl.canvas[1]);
  tpl.draw(cx, tpl.canvas[0], tpl.canvas[1]);
  cx.restore();
  return c.toDataURL();
}

function renderTemplateGrid(){
  tplGrid.innerHTML = '';
  TEMPLATES.forEach(tpl=>{
    const card = document.createElement('div');
    card.className = 'tpl-card' + (tpl.id===state.template.id ? ' active':'');
    card.dataset.id = tpl.id;
    const img = document.createElement('img');
    img.src = buildTemplateThumb(tpl);
    img.style.width='100%'; img.style.height='100%'; img.style.objectFit='cover';
    card.appendChild(img);
    const label = document.createElement('div');
    label.className = 'tpl-label';
    label.textContent = tpl.name;
    card.appendChild(label);
    const dims = document.createElement('div');
    dims.className = 'tpl-dims';
    dims.textContent = tpl.canvas[0]+'×'+tpl.canvas[1];
    card.appendChild(dims);
    if(tpl.turntable){
      const badge = document.createElement('div');
      badge.className = 'tpl-360-badge';
      badge.textContent = '360°';
      card.appendChild(badge);
    }
    card.addEventListener('click', ()=>selectTemplate(tpl.id));
    tplGrid.appendChild(card);
  });
}

function updateCornersForView() {
  const tpl = state.template;
  const key = tpl.id + '_' + state.view;
  if (state.customCorners[key]) {
    state.corners = state.customCorners[key].map(p=>p.slice());
    return;
  }
  
  if (state.view === 'front' && tpl.cornersFront) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersFront.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'side' && tpl.cornersSide) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersSide.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'back' && tpl.cornersBack) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersBack.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'back' && tpl.cornersFront) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersFront.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'other_side' && tpl.cornersOtherSide) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersOtherSide.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'other_side' && tpl.cornersSide) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersSide.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else if (state.view === 'top' && tpl.cornersTop) {
    state.corners = tpl.cornersTop.map(p=>p.slice());
  } else {
    state.corners = tpl.corners.map(p=>p.slice());
  }
}

function selectTemplate(id){
  const tpl = TEMPLATES.find(t=>t.id===id);
  if(!tpl) return;
  state.template = tpl;
  state.blend = tpl.blend;
  state.opacity = tpl.opacity;
  opacitySlider.value = Math.round(tpl.opacity*100);
  opacityVal.textContent = Math.round(tpl.opacity*100)+'%';
  [...blendSeg.children].forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.mode===tpl.blend));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tpl-card').forEach(c=>c.classList.toggle('active', c.dataset.id===id));
  metaTpl.textContent = tpl.id;
  metaCanvas.textContent = tpl.canvas[0]+'×'+tpl.canvas[1];
  metaBlend.textContent = tpl.blend;
  stageTplName.textContent = tpl.name;

  stopTurntableSpin();
  state.ttAngle = 0;
  ttSlider.value = 0;
  ttDeg.textContent = '0°';
  
  // Invalidate dieline cache so panel ratios are recomputed for new template
  _dielineCache = { src: null, tplId: null, layout: null };
  if (state.dielineMode && state.designImg) {
    renderDielinePreview();
  }

  // Auto-fit template dimensions to match design aspect ratio
  if (state.designImg && typeof buildDimPanel === 'function') {
    buildDimPanel(tpl);
    if (typeof matchAspectRatio === 'function') matchAspectRatio();
  }
  
  const extraViews = ['side','back','other_side','top'];
  [...viewSeg.children].forEach(b=>{
    const view = b.dataset.view;
    const isSupported = (view==='3d' || view==='front' || (tpl.turntable && extraViews.includes(view)));
    b.disabled = !isSupported;
    b.classList.toggle('disabled', !isSupported);
  });
  
  const isCurrentViewSupported = (state.view==='3d' || state.view==='front' || (tpl.turntable && extraViews.includes(state.view)));
  setView(isCurrentViewSupported ? state.view : '3d');
}

function setView(view){
  state.view = view;
  [...viewSeg.children].forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('active', b.dataset.view===view));
  
  const is3D = (view === '3d');
  const isTurntable = state.template.turntable;
  
  turntableBar.style.display = (is3D && isTurntable) ? 'flex' : 'none';
  pinToggle.style.display = is3D ? 'none' : 'flex';
  frameSeqBtn.style.display = (is3D && isTurntable) ? 'flex' : 'none';
  resetBtn.style.display = is3D ? 'none' : 'flex';
  
  if(!is3D) stopTurntableSpin();
  
  updateCornersForView();
  renderStage();
}

viewSeg.addEventListener('click', e=>{
  const btn = e.target.closest('button'); if(!btn || btn.disabled) return;
  const view = btn.dataset.view;
  setView(view);
});

ttSlider.addEventListener('input', e=>{
  stopTurntableSpin();
  state.ttAngle = Number(e.target.value);
  ttDeg.textContent = state.ttAngle+'°';
  renderStage();
});

ttPlayBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  if(state.ttPlaying) stopTurntableSpin();
  else startTurntableSpin();
});

function startTurntableSpin(){
  state.ttPlaying = true;
  ttPlayIcon.style.display='none';
  ttPauseIcon.style.display='block';
  state.ttLastTs = null;
  const step = (ts)=>{
    if(!state.ttPlaying) return;
    if(state.ttLastTs!=null){
      const dt = ts - state.ttLastTs;
      state.ttAngle = (state.ttAngle + dt*0.05) % 360;
      ttSlider.value = Math.round(state.ttAngle);
      ttDeg.textContent = Math.round(state.ttAngle)+'°';
      renderStage();
    }
    state.ttLastTs = ts;
    state.ttRafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
  };
  state.ttRafId = requestAnimationFrame(step);
}

function stopTurntableSpin(){
  state.ttPlaying = false;
  ttPlayIcon.style.display='block';
  ttPauseIcon.style.display='none';
  if(state.ttRafId){ cancelAnimationFrame(state.ttRafId); state.ttRafId=null; }
  state.ttLastTs = null;
}

/* =========================================================
   STAGE RENDER — perspective warp via homography + composite
   ========================================================= */

function computeHomography(srcW, srcH, dst){
  const s = [[0,0],[srcW,0],[srcW,srcH],[0,srcH]];
  const d = dst;
  const A = [];
  const b = [];
  for(let i=0;i<4;i++){
    const [x,y] = s[i];
    const [X,Y] = d[i];
    A.push([x,y,1,0,0,0,-x*X,-y*X]); b.push(X);
    A.push([0,0,0,x,y,1,-x*Y,-y*Y]); b.push(Y);
  }
  const h = solveLinear(A,b);
  return [h[0],h[1],h[2], h[3],h[4],h[5], h[6],h[7],1];
}

function solveLinear(A,b){
  const n = 8;
  const M = A.map((row,i)=>[...row,b[i]]);
  for(let col=0; col<n; col++){
    let pivot = col;
    for(let r=col+1;r<n;r++) if(Math.abs(M[r][col])>Math.abs(M[pivot][col])) pivot=r;
    [M[col],M[pivot]] = [M[pivot],M[col]];
    const pv = M[col][col] || 1e-12;
    for(let c=col;c<=n;c++) M[col][c] /= pv;
    for(let r=0;r<n;r++){
      if(r===col) continue;
      const factor = M[r][col];
      for(let c=col;c<=n;c++) M[r][c] -= factor*M[col][c];
    }
  }
  return M.map(row=>row[n]);
}

function drawWarpedImage(destCtx, img, srcW, srcH, dstQuad){
  const H = computeHomography(srcW, srcH, dstQuad);
  const cols = 32, rows = 32;
  const stepX = srcW/cols, stepY = srcH/rows;

  function mapPt(x,y){
    const X = H[0]*x + H[1]*y + H[2];
    const Y = H[3]*x + H[4]*y + H[5];
    const W = H[6]*x + H[7]*y + H[8];
    return [X/W, Y/W];
  }

  destCtx.save();
  destCtx.beginPath();
  destCtx.moveTo(...dstQuad[0]);
  destCtx.lineTo(...dstQuad[1]);
  destCtx.lineTo(...dstQuad[2]);
  destCtx.lineTo(...dstQuad[3]);
  destCtx.closePath();
  destCtx.clip();

  for(let j=0;j<rows;j++){
    for(let i=0;i<cols;i++){
      const sx0=i*stepX, sy0=j*stepY, sx1=sx0+stepX, sy1=sy0+stepY;
      const p00 = mapPt(sx0,sy0), p10 = mapPt(sx1,sy0), p11 = mapPt(sx1,sy1), p01 = mapPt(sx0,sy1);
      drawTriangle(destCtx,img, sx0,sy0,sx1,sy0,sx1,sy1, p00,p10,p11);
      drawTriangle(destCtx,img, sx0,sy0,sx1,sy1,sx0,sy1, p00,p11,p01);
    }
  }
  destCtx.restore();
}

function drawTriangle(ctx,img, sx0,sy0,sx1,sy1,sx2,sy2, d0,d1,d2){
  ctx.save();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(d0[0],d0[1]); ctx.lineTo(d1[0],d1[1]); ctx.lineTo(d2[0],d2[1]);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.clip();

  const denom = (sx1-sx0)*(sy2-sy0) - (sx2-sx0)*(sy1-sy0);
  if(Math.abs(denom) < 1e-8){ ctx.restore(); return; }

  const a = ((d1[0]-d0[0])*(sy2-sy0) - (d2[0]-d0[0])*(sy1-sy0))/denom;
  const b = ((d2[0]-d0[0])*(sx1-sx0) - (d1[0]-d0[0])*(sx2-sx0))/denom;
  const c = ((d1[1]-d0[1])*(sy2-sy0) - (d2[1]-d0[1])*(sy1-sy0))/denom;
  const d = ((d2[1]-d0[1])*(sx1-sx0) - (d1[1]-d0[1])*(sx2-sx0))/denom;
  const e = d0[0] - a*sx0 - b*sy0;
  const f = d0[1] - c*sx0 - d*sy0;

  ctx.transform(a,c,b,d,e,f);
  ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true;
  ctx.drawImage(img,0,0);
  ctx.restore();
}

function fitDimensions(imgW, imgH, quad, mode){
  const xs = quad.map(p=>p[0]), ys = quad.map(p=>p[1]);
  const bw = Math.max(...xs)-Math.min(...xs);
  const bh = Math.max(...ys)-Math.min(...ys);
  if(mode==='stretch') return {w:imgW,h:imgH};
  const scale = mode==='cover'
    ? Math.max(bw/imgW, bh/imgH)
    : Math.min(bw/imgW, bh/imgH);
  return {w:bw/scale, h:bh/scale};
}

/* =========================================================
   DIELINE AUTO-DETECTION ENGINE  (v2 — template-aware)
   ========================================================= */

let _dielineCache = { src: null, tplId: null, layout: null };
let _manualDielineOverride = null; // { srcKey, bodyBox, splitXs, topBox } in image-pixel coords, or null when using auto-detection

function analyzeDielineLayout(img) {
  const isGenMockActive = document.getElementById('page-genmock') && document.getElementById('page-genmock').classList.contains('active');
  const tplId = isGenMockActive 
    ? 'gm-' + (window.gmSelectedShape || 'box')
    : (state.template ? state.template.id : null);

  if (_dielineCache.src === img.src && _dielineCache.tplId === tplId && _dielineCache.layout) {
    return _dielineCache.layout;
  }
  const layout = _detectPanelBoundaries(img);
  _dielineCache = { src: img.src, tplId, layout };
  return layout;
}

// ── Adaptive background sampler ──────────────────────────────────────────────
// Samples corners + a grid of edge pixels to robustly determine bg color
// even when corners are partially covered by artwork bleed.
function _sampleBgColor(data, w, h) {
  const samplePts = [
    [0,0],[w-1,0],[0,h-1],[w-1,h-1],
    [Math.floor(w/2),0],[Math.floor(w/2),h-1],
    [0,Math.floor(h/2)],[w-1,Math.floor(h/2)]
  ];
  let r=0,g=0,b=0,a=0,n=0;
  samplePts.forEach(([x,y])=>{
    const i=(y*w+x)*4;
    r+=data[i]; g+=data[i+1]; b+=data[i+2]; a+=data[i+3]; n++;
  });
  return {r:r/n, g:g/n, b:b/n, a:a/n};
}

function detectDielineContentBox(img) {
  const w = img.width, h = img.height;
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  canvas.width = w; canvas.height = h;
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
  const imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h);
  const data = imgData.data;
  const bg = _sampleBgColor(data, w, h);

  // Dynamic threshold: looser for semi-transparent images
  const hasAlpha = bg.a < 200;
  const thresh = hasAlpha ? 15 : 28;

  let minX=w, maxX=0, minY=h, maxY=0;
  for (let y=0;y<h;y++) {
    for (let x=0;x<w;x++) {
      const idx=(y*w+x)*4;
      const r=data[idx],g=data[idx+1],b=data[idx+2],a=data[idx+3];
      const colorDist=Math.sqrt((r-bg.r)**2+(g-bg.g)**2+(b-bg.b)**2);
      const alphaDist=Math.abs(a-bg.a);
      if (colorDist>thresh || alphaDist>thresh) {
        if(x<minX)minX=x; if(x>maxX)maxX=x;
        if(y<minY)minY=y; if(y>maxY)maxY=y;
      }
    }
  }
  if (maxX<minX||maxY<minY||(maxX-minX<10)||(maxY-minY<10)) return {x:0,y:0,w,h};
  minX=Math.max(0,minX-2); minY=Math.max(0,minY-2);
  maxX=Math.min(w-1,maxX+2); maxY=Math.min(h-1,maxY+2);
  return {x:minX,y:minY,w:maxX-minX+1,h:maxY-minY+1};
}

// Builds a boolean content mask for the whole image (true = non-background pixel),
// used to separate the dieline into independent artwork blocks rather than relying
// on a single merged bounding box, which breaks layouts where the top-flap panel
// is a physically separate piece of art positioned beside/above the main strip.
function _buildDielineContentMask(img) {
  const w = img.width, h = img.height;
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  canvas.width = w; canvas.height = h;
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
  const imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h);
  const data = imgData.data;
  const bg = _sampleBgColor(data, w, h);
  const hasAlpha = bg.a < 200;
  const thresh = hasAlpha ? 15 : 28;

  const mask = new Uint8Array(w * h);
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) {
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
      const idx = (y * w + x) * 4;
      const r=data[idx],g=data[idx+1],b=data[idx+2],a=data[idx+3];
      const colorDist=Math.sqrt((r-bg.r)**2+(g-bg.g)**2+(b-bg.b)**2);
      const alphaDist=Math.abs(a-bg.a);
      if (colorDist>thresh || alphaDist>thresh) mask[y*w+x]=1;
    }
  }
  return { mask, w, h };
}

// Finds the bounding box of content within mask rows [yStart, yEnd) and
// columns [xStart, xEnd). Returns null if no content found.
//
// Uses column/row content-density projections rather than raw pixel min/max:
// a single stray pixel (e.g. a JPEG compression artifact far from the real
// artwork) would otherwise blow out the whole box to that pixel's position.
// Real panel edges have many masked pixels stacked in their column/row;
// noise has very few. Columns/rows are only counted as "content" once their
// pixel count clears a small threshold relative to the region's own peak
// density, so isolated noise pixels are ignored.
function _maskBBoxIn(maskInfo, xStart, xEnd, yStart, yEnd) {
  const { mask, w } = maskInfo;
  const regionW = xEnd - xStart, regionH = yEnd - yStart;
  if (regionW <= 0 || regionH <= 0) return null;

  const colCount = new Array(regionW).fill(0);
  const rowCount = new Array(regionH).fill(0);
  for (let y = yStart; y < yEnd; y++) {
    const rowBase = y * w;
    let rc = 0;
    for (let x = xStart; x < xEnd; x++) {
      if (mask[rowBase + x]) { colCount[x - xStart]++; rc++; }
    }
    rowCount[y - yStart] = rc;
  }

  const maxCol = Math.max(...colCount);
  const maxRow = Math.max(...rowCount);
  if (maxCol === 0 || maxRow === 0) return null;

  // A real edge of the artwork has a run of columns/rows with a non-trivial
  // pixel count. Threshold at 1% of the region's peak density (with a floor
  // of 2px) — enough to drop single stray pixels while keeping any genuine,
  // even if thin, content band.
  const colThresh = Math.max(2, maxCol * 0.01);
  const rowThresh = Math.max(2, maxRow * 0.01);

  let minX = -1, maxX = -1;
  for (let i = 0; i < regionW; i++) {
    if (colCount[i] >= colThresh) { if (minX === -1) minX = i; maxX = i; }
  }
  let minY = -1, maxY = -1;
  for (let i = 0; i < regionH; i++) {
    if (rowCount[i] >= rowThresh) { if (minY === -1) minY = i; maxY = i; }
  }

  if (minX === -1 || minY === -1) return null;
  return { x: xStart + minX, y: yStart + minY, w: maxX - minX + 1, h: maxY - minY + 1 };
}

// Detects the dieline's body-strip block (front/side/back/other_side, the widest
// horizontal content band) and, separately, a top-flap block if one exists above
// or beside it as an independent piece of art. Falls back to a single merged
// box (old behavior) if the layout doesn't look like two separate pieces.
function detectDielineBlocks(img) {
  const w = img.width, h = img.height;
  const maskInfo = _buildDielineContentMask(img);
  const { mask } = maskInfo;

  // Row-wise content width (how many non-bg pixels in each row).
  const rowWidth = new Array(h).fill(0);
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) {
    let count = 0;
    const rowBase = y * w;
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) count += mask[rowBase + x];
    rowWidth[y] = count;
  }

  const overall = _maskBBoxIn(maskInfo, 0, w, 0, h);
  if (!overall) return { body: { x: 0, y: 0, w, h }, top: null };

  // The body strip is identified as the band of rows whose content width is
  // close to the image's maximum content width (i.e. spans nearly the full
  // strip). Any rows above that band with a much narrower content width
  // belong to a separate top-flap block, not the body strip.
  const maxRowWidth = Math.max(...rowWidth);
  const wideThresh = maxRowWidth * 0.6;

  let bodyStartY = overall.y;
  for (let y = overall.y; y <= overall.y + overall.h; y++) {
    if (rowWidth[y] >= wideThresh) { bodyStartY = y; break; }
  }

  if (bodyStartY <= overall.y + 2) {
    // No separate narrow band above the body — single unified block.
    return { body: overall, top: null };
  }

  const bodyBox = _maskBBoxIn(maskInfo, 0, w, bodyStartY, overall.y + overall.h + 1);
  const topBox  = _maskBBoxIn(maskInfo, 0, w, overall.y, bodyStartY);

  if (!bodyBox) return { body: overall, top: null };
  return { body: bodyBox, top: topBox };
}

function getTemplateFaceRatios(tpl) {
  const getQuadWidth = (quad) => {
    if (!quad) return 0;
    const wTop = Math.abs(quad[1][0] - quad[0][0]);
    const wBot = Math.abs(quad[2][0] - quad[3][0]);
    return (wTop + wBot) / 2;
  };
  const wFront = getQuadWidth(tpl.cornersFront || tpl.corners);
  const wSide = getQuadWidth(tpl.cornersSide || tpl.corners);
  const wBack = getQuadWidth(tpl.cornersBack || tpl.corners);
  const wOtherSide = getQuadWidth(tpl.cornersOtherSide || tpl.corners);
  
  const total = wFront + wSide + wBack + wOtherSide;
  if (total <= 0) {
    return [0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25];
  }
  return [wFront / total, wSide / total, wBack / total, wOtherSide / total];
}

// ── Smart column gap finder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Scans the body strip for natural vertical "crease" lines using THREE strategies:
//
//  1. EMPTY GAP scan   — columns where many pixels are background-colored.
//                        Works on dielines that have white/transparent fold lines.
//
//  2. COLOR EDGE scan  — columns where adjacent pixel colors change abruptly
//                        (horizontal gradient magnitude peaks). Fold creases cause
//                        a sudden color shift even when both panels are fully filled.
//                        Renders the body strip to a small canvas for speed.
//
//  3. LOCAL MINIMA     — fallback relative-minimum search on the emptiness profile.
//
// Returns an array of absolute x positions (image coords) sorted left→right.
function _findVerticalGaps(img, bodyBox, maskInfo) {
  const { mask, w: IW } = maskInfo;
  const bx = bodyBox.x, by = bodyBox.y, bw = bodyBox.w, bh = bodyBox.h;

  // ── Strategy 1: empty-column scan (classic approach) ──────────────────────
  const colEmpty = new Float32Array(bw);
  for (let col = 0; col < bw; col++) {
    let empty = 0;
    for (let row = 0; row < bh; row++) {
      if (!mask[(by + row) * IW + (bx + col)]) empty++;
    }
    colEmpty[col] = empty / bh;
  }

  const smooth = 8;
  const smoothedEmpty = new Float32Array(bw);
  for (let i = 0; i < bw; i++) {
    let s = 0, c = 0;
    for (let k = -smooth; k <= smooth; k++) {
      const j = i + k;
      if (j >= 0 && j < bw) { s += colEmpty[j]; c++; }
    }
    smoothedEmpty[i] = s / c;
  }

  const GAP_THRESH = 0.35;
  const gapCols = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < bw - 1; i++) {
    if (smoothedEmpty[i] >= GAP_THRESH &&
        smoothedEmpty[i] >= smoothedEmpty[i-1] &&
        smoothedEmpty[i] >= smoothedEmpty[i+1]) {
      gapCols.push(i);
    }
  }

  const mergeRadius = Math.round(bw * 0.05);
  const merged = _mergeGapCols(gapCols, mergeRadius, bx);

  if (merged.length > 0) return merged;

  // ── Strategy 2: horizontal color-edge scan ─────────────────────────────────
  // Render body strip to a small canvas (max 512px wide) for fast pixel access.
  // Compute per-column mean horizontal gradient magnitude — peaks correspond to
  // fold creases where adjacent panels have different dominant colors.
  try {
    const SCAN_W = Math.min(bw, 512);
    const SCAN_H = Math.min(bh, 256);
    const sc = SCAN_W / bw;
    const sc_h = SCAN_H / bh;
    const scanCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    scanCanvas.width = SCAN_W; scanCanvas.height = SCAN_H;
    const sctx = scanCanvas.getContext('2d');
    sctx.drawImage(img, bx, by, bw, bh, 0, 0, SCAN_W, SCAN_H);
    const pixels = sctx.getImageData(0, 0, SCAN_W, SCAN_H).data;

    // Build column horizontal gradient magnitude profile
    const edgeProfile = new Float32Array(SCAN_W);
    for (let x = 1; x < SCAN_W - 1; x++) {
      let sumGrad = 0;
      for (let y = 0; y < SCAN_H; y++) {
        const iL = (y * SCAN_W + x - 1) * 4;
        const iR = (y * SCAN_W + x + 1) * 4;
        const aL = pixels[iL + 3], aR = pixels[iR + 3];
        if (aL < 20 || aR < 20) continue; // skip transparent
        const dr = pixels[iR] - pixels[iL];
        const dg = pixels[iR+1] - pixels[iL+1];
        const db = pixels[iR+2] - pixels[iL+2];
        sumGrad += Math.sqrt(dr*dr + dg*dg + db*db);
      }
      edgeProfile[x] = sumGrad / Math.max(1, SCAN_H);
    }

    // Smooth edge profile with 5px window
    const smoothedEdge = new Float32Array(SCAN_W);
    for (let i = 0; i < SCAN_W; i++) {
      let s = 0, c = 0;
      for (let k = -5; k <= 5; k++) {
        const j = i + k;
        if (j >= 0 && j < SCAN_W) { s += edgeProfile[j]; c++; }
      }
      smoothedEdge[i] = s / c;
    }

    // Find local maxima above a meaningful threshold
    const maxEdge = Math.max(...smoothedEdge);
    const edgeThresh = maxEdge * 0.35; // must be at least 35% of the strongest edge
    const edgePeaks = [];
    const margin = Math.round(SCAN_W * 0.06); // ignore outer 6%
    for (let i = margin; i < SCAN_W - margin; i++) {
      if (smoothedEdge[i] > edgeThresh &&
          smoothedEdge[i] >= smoothedEdge[i-1] &&
          smoothedEdge[i] >= smoothedEdge[i+1]) {
        edgePeaks.push(i);
      }
    }

    // Convert back to body-strip pixel coords and merge nearby peaks
    const edgeMergeR = Math.round(SCAN_W * 0.05);
    const edgePeaksMerged = _mergeGapCols(edgePeaks, edgeMergeR, 0)
      .map(x => bx + Math.round(x / sc));

    if (edgePeaksMerged.length > 0) return edgePeaksMerged;
  } catch(e) { /* canvas tainted or unavailable — fall through */ }

  // ── Strategy 3: local minima of emptiness profile ─────────────────────────
  const s3Cols = [];
  for (let col = 4; col < bw - 4; col++) {
    const localMin = smoothedEmpty[col] <= smoothedEmpty[col-1] &&
                     smoothedEmpty[col] <= smoothedEmpty[col+1];
    const localMin3 = smoothedEmpty[col] <= smoothedEmpty[col-3] &&
                      smoothedEmpty[col] <= smoothedEmpty[col+3];
    const avgNeighbour = (smoothedEmpty[col-4] + smoothedEmpty[col-3] +
                          smoothedEmpty[col+3] + smoothedEmpty[col+4]) / 4;
    if (localMin && localMin3 && (avgNeighbour - smoothedEmpty[col]) >= 0.04) {
      s3Cols.push(col);
    }
  }
  const mergeR3 = Math.round(bw * 0.05);
  const merged3 = _mergeGapCols(s3Cols, mergeR3, bx);
  return merged3;
}

// Helper: merge nearby gap column indices and convert to absolute image x coords
function _mergeGapCols(cols, mergeRadius, offsetX) {
  if (cols.length === 0) return [];
  const result = [];
  let i = 0;
  while (i < cols.length) {
    let j = i;
    while (j + 1 < cols.length && cols[j+1] - cols[j] <= mergeRadius) j++;
    const centre = Math.round((cols[i] + cols[j]) / 2);
    result.push(offsetX + centre);
    i = j + 1;
  }
  return result;
}

// ── Template-guided split correction ────────────────────────────────────────
// If gap detection found the wrong number of gaps, fall back to template ratios
// anchored at the auto-detected body box so at least the outer bounds are right.
function _splitByRatios(bodyBox, ratios, W) {
  const clamp = (v, lo, hi) => Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, Math.round(v)));
  const { x: bx, w: bw } = bodyBox;
  const splits = [];
  let cursor = bx;
  for (let i = 0; i < ratios.length - 1; i++) {
    cursor += bw * ratios[i];
    splits.push(clamp(cursor, 0, W - 1));
  }
  return splits;
}

// ── Content-weighted panel split ─────────────────────────────────────────────
// When pixel gap detection finds no clear fold lines AND edge scan was insufficient,
// this function divides the body strip into `nSplits + 1` segments by finding
// columns that have:
//   (a) the most abrupt horizontal color change (edge detection), OR
//   (b) the most color-homogeneous column (least variance = most "fold-like")
// Combines both signals to rank candidate split positions.
// Returns an array of `nSplits` absolute x positions, or null if inconclusive.
function _contentWeightedSplit(img, bodyBox, maskInfo, nSplits) {
  if (!maskInfo || nSplits < 1) return null;
  const { mask, w: IW } = maskInfo;
  const bx = bodyBox.x, by = bodyBox.y, bw = bodyBox.w, bh = bodyBox.h;
  if (bw < nSplits * 8) return null;

  // Try color-edge approach first using a scan canvas
  try {
    const SCAN_W = Math.min(bw, 512);
    const SCAN_H = Math.min(bh, 256);
    const sc = SCAN_W / bw;
    const scanCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    scanCanvas.width = SCAN_W; scanCanvas.height = SCAN_H;
    const sctx = scanCanvas.getContext('2d');
    sctx.drawImage(img, bx, by, bw, bh, 0, 0, SCAN_W, SCAN_H);
    const pixels = sctx.getImageData(0, 0, SCAN_W, SCAN_H).data;

    // Compute horizontal gradient magnitude per column
    const edgeProfile = new Float32Array(SCAN_W);
    for (let x = 1; x < SCAN_W - 1; x++) {
      let sumGrad = 0, count = 0;
      for (let y = 0; y < SCAN_H; y++) {
        const iL = (y * SCAN_W + x - 1) * 4;
        const iR = (y * SCAN_W + x + 1) * 4;
        if (pixels[iL+3] < 20 || pixels[iR+3] < 20) continue;
        const dr = pixels[iR] - pixels[iL];
        const dg = pixels[iR+1] - pixels[iL+1];
        const db = pixels[iR+2] - pixels[iL+2];
        sumGrad += Math.sqrt(dr*dr + dg*dg + db*db);
        count++;
      }
      edgeProfile[x] = count > 0 ? sumGrad / count : 0;
    }

    // Smooth
    const smoothedEdge = new Float32Array(SCAN_W);
    for (let i = 0; i < SCAN_W; i++) {
      let s = 0, c = 0;
      for (let k = -6; k <= 6; k++) {
        const j = i + k;
        if (j >= 0 && j < SCAN_W) { s += edgeProfile[j]; c++; }
      }
      smoothedEdge[i] = s / c;
    }

    // Collect local maxima as candidate split positions
    const margin = Math.round(SCAN_W * 0.10);
    const candidates = [];
    for (let i = margin; i < SCAN_W - margin; i++) {
      if (smoothedEdge[i] >= smoothedEdge[i-1] && smoothedEdge[i] >= smoothedEdge[i+1]) {
        candidates.push({ x: i, e: smoothedEdge[i] });
      }
    }
    // Sort by edge magnitude descending (strongest edge = most likely crease)
    candidates.sort((a, b) => b.e - a.e);

    const minSpacing = Math.round(SCAN_W * 0.10);
    const chosen = [];
    for (const c of candidates) {
      if (chosen.length >= nSplits) break;
      const tooClose = chosen.some(s => Math.abs(s.x - c.x) < minSpacing);
      if (!tooClose) chosen.push(c);
    }

    if (chosen.length === nSplits) {
      chosen.sort((a, b) => a.x - b.x);
      return chosen.map(c => bx + Math.round(c.x / sc));
    }
  } catch(e) { /* fall through to density-based */ }

  // Fallback: column density (original approach)
  const colEnergy = new Float32Array(bw);
  for (let col = 0; col < bw; col++) {
    let filled = 0;
    for (let row = 0; row < bh; row++) {
      if (mask[(by + row) * IW + (bx + col)]) filled++;
    }
    colEnergy[col] = filled / Math.max(1, bh);
  }

  const smoothed = new Float32Array(bw);
  for (let i = 0; i < bw; i++) {
    let s = 0, c = 0;
    for (let k = -5; k <= 5; k++) {
      const j = i + k;
      if (j >= 0 && j < bw) { s += colEnergy[j]; c++; }
    }
    smoothed[i] = s / c;
  }

  const margin = Math.round(bw * 0.10);
  const candidates = [];
  for (let i = margin; i < bw - margin; i++) {
    candidates.push({ x: i, e: smoothed[i] });
  }
  candidates.sort((a, b) => a.e - b.e);

  const minSpacing = Math.round(bw * 0.08);
  const chosen = [];
  for (const c of candidates) {
    if (chosen.length >= nSplits) break;
    const tooClose = chosen.some(s => Math.abs(s.x - c.x) < minSpacing);
    if (!tooClose) chosen.push(c);
  }

  if (chosen.length !== nSplits) return null;
  chosen.sort((a, b) => a.x - b.x);
  return chosen.map(c => bx + c.x);
}

function _detectPanelBoundaries(img) {
  const W = img.width, H = img.height;
  // A person can drag the split lines in the "Detected Panels" preview to
  // correct a wrong automatic split (e.g. when the source image has no real
  // fold-line gaps for the detector to find, like a photographed hero shot
  // instead of a flat dieline). When that's happened for this exact image,
  // use their corrected values instead of re-running detection.
  const manual = (_manualDielineOverride && _manualDielineOverride.srcKey === img.src) ? _manualDielineOverride : null;

  const blocks = detectDielineBlocks(img);
  const bodyBox = (manual && manual.bodyBox) ? manual.bodyBox : blocks.body;
  const topBox  = manual ? manual.topBox : blocks.top;

  let tpl = state.template;
  const isGenMockActive = document.getElementById('page-genmock') && document.getElementById('page-genmock').classList.contains('active');
  if (isGenMockActive) {
    const shape = window.gmSelectedShape || 'box';
    let tplId = 'tshirt-front-01';
    if (shape === 'box') tplId = 'box-rect-01';
    else if (shape === 'bottle') tplId = 'bottle-01';
    else if (shape === 'bag') tplId = 'tote-01';
    else if (shape === 'tshirt') tplId = 'tshirt-front-01';
    else if (shape === 'can') tplId = 'tin-can-01';
    else if (shape === 'pouch') tplId = 'sachet-01';
    tpl = TEMPLATES.find(t => t.id === tplId) || TEMPLATES[0];
  }

  const rig  = tpl.rig; // 'box' | 'sachet' | undefined
  const isSachet = rig === 'sachet';

  const clamp = (v, lo, hi) => Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, v));

  const sideTopY = clamp(bodyBox.y, 0, H);
  const sideBotY = clamp(bodyBox.y + bodyBox.h, 0, H);
  const sideH    = Math.max(1, sideBotY - sideTopY);

  // ── Vertical gap detection ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const maskInfo = _buildDielineContentMask(img);
  const detectedGaps = manual ? [] : _findVerticalGaps(img, bodyBox, maskInfo);

  // Expected number of internal splits
  // Sachet: 1 split (front | back)
  // Box: 3 splits (front | side | back | other_side)
  const expectedSplits = isSachet ? 1 : 3;
  const ratios = getTemplateFaceRatios(tpl);

  let splitXs; // absolute x of each internal boundary
  if (manual && manual.splitXs) {
    splitXs = manual.splitXs;
  } else if (detectedGaps.length === expectedSplits) {
    splitXs = detectedGaps;
  } else if (detectedGaps.length > expectedSplits) {
    // More gaps than expected — keep the N gaps that best match template-ratio
    // predictions. For ties, prefer gaps that are more evenly spaced.
    const ratioBased = _splitByRatios(bodyBox, ratios, W);
    splitXs = ratioBased.map(rx => {
      let best = detectedGaps[0], bestD = Math.abs(detectedGaps[0] - rx);
      detectedGaps.forEach(gx => { const d = Math.abs(gx - rx); if (d < bestD) { bestD = d; best = gx; }});
      return best;
    });
    // Deduplicate (in case two ratio points snap to same gap)
    splitXs = [...new Set(splitXs)].sort((a, b) => a - b);
    // If deduplication left fewer than expected, pad with ratio-based splits
    if (splitXs.length < expectedSplits) {
      ratioBased.forEach(rx => {
        if (splitXs.length < expectedSplits && !splitXs.some(x => Math.abs(x - rx) < bodyBox.w * 0.04)) {
          splitXs.push(rx);
        }
      });
      splitXs.sort((a, b) => a - b);
    }
  } else {
    // Fewer gaps than expected – try a content-aware column energy split first.
    // Divides the body strip into N segments weighted by column content density,
    // so that heavier-artwork panels (front) get more width than lighter ones (sides).
    // Falls back to equal template ratios if content-weight scan is inconclusive.
    const contentSplits = _contentWeightedSplit(img, bodyBox, maskInfo, expectedSplits);
    if (contentSplits && contentSplits.length === expectedSplits) {
      splitXs = contentSplits;
    } else {
      splitXs = _splitByRatios(bodyBox, ratios, W);
    }
  }

  // Build panel rects from body-box left edge through each split to right edge
  const panelXs = [bodyBox.x, ...splitXs, bodyBox.x + bodyBox.w];
  const panels = panelXs.slice(0, -1).map((x0, i) => ({
    x: clamp(x0, 0, W),
    y: sideTopY,
    w: clamp(panelXs[i + 1] - x0, 1, W - clamp(x0, 0, W)),
    h: sideH
  }));

  // ── Border strip extraction ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  let borderStripCanvas = null;
  try {
    const stripW = _detectBorderStripWidth(img, bodyBox);
    if (stripW > 0) {
      borderStripCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      borderStripCanvas.width  = stripW;
      borderStripCanvas.height = bodyBox.h;
      const sctx = borderStripCanvas.getContext('2d');
      sctx.drawImage(img, bodyBox.x, bodyBox.y, stripW, bodyBox.h, 0, 0, stripW, bodyBox.h);
    }
  } catch(e) { borderStripCanvas = null; }

  // ── Assemble result ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const result = {
    _bodyBox:   bodyBox,
    _borderStripCanvas: borderStripCanvas,
    _splitXs: splitXs,   // expose detected splits for preview rendering
    _detectedGaps: detectedGaps,
    _edgeDetected: detectedGaps.length === 0 && splitXs && splitXs.length > 0,
    _manualOverride: !!manual
  };

  if (isSachet) {
    result.front = panels[0] || { x: bodyBox.x, y: sideTopY, w: Math.round(bodyBox.w * 0.5), h: sideH };
    result.back  = panels[1] || { x: bodyBox.x + Math.round(bodyBox.w * 0.5), y: sideTopY, w: Math.round(bodyBox.w * 0.5), h: sideH };
  } else {
    const faceOrder = ['front', 'side', 'back', 'other_side'];
    panels.forEach((p, i) => {
      if (i < faceOrder.length && p.w > 0) result[faceOrder[i]] = p;
    });
  }

  // ── Top panel ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (topBox) {
    result.top = { x: topBox.x, y: topBox.y, w: topBox.w, h: topBox.h, rotate: true };
  } else if (!isSachet && !manual) {
    let rTopHeight = 0;
    if (tpl.cornersTop) {
      const getQuadHeight = (quad) => {
        if (!quad) return 0;
        const hLeft  = Math.abs(quad[3][1] - quad[0][1]);
        const hRight = Math.abs(quad[2][1] - quad[1][1]);
        return (hLeft + hRight) / 2;
      };
      const hFront = getQuadHeight(tpl.cornersFront || tpl.corners);
      const hTop   = getQuadHeight(tpl.cornersTop);
      if (hFront + hTop > 0) rTopHeight = hTop / (hFront + hTop);
    }
    if (rTopHeight > 0 && result.front) {
      const frontPanel = result.front;
      const fallbackH = Math.max(1, Math.round(sideH * rTopHeight / Math.max(0.0001, 1 - rTopHeight)));
      result.top = { x: frontPanel.x, y: Math.max(0, sideTopY - fallbackH), w: frontPanel.w, h: fallbackH, rotate: true };
    }
  }

  return result;
}

// Returns the width of the decorative vertical border strip on the body
// strip's genuine left edge (the real, unaltered edge of the artwork).
// A fixed proportion of the body strip's width is used rather than
// per-image color-edge detection: dieline border art varies too much
// (rope patterns, gradients, illustration bleed near the edge) for a
// generic color-distance scan to reliably find the true border boundary,
// and a wrong guess there would crop into real artwork. This ratio is
// calibrated against typical dieline border proportions and clamped to a
// sane pixel range.
function _detectBorderStripWidth(img, bodyBox) {
  const ratio = 0.016; // ~1.6% of body strip width
  let stripW = Math.round(bodyBox.w * ratio);
  stripW = Math.max(12, Math.min(60, stripW));
  return stripW;
}

// Stamps a copy of the genuine left-edge border strip onto a synthetic edge
// (left or right side of a panel that was cut out of the middle of the
// artwork, where no printed border exists). The original artwork pixels are
// never modified — this only affects the small extracted panel canvas drawn
// for 3D compositing, so the source dieline image stays untouched.
function _stampBorderStrip(panelCanvas, borderStripCanvas, side) {
  const pctx = panelCanvas.getContext('2d');
  const bw = borderStripCanvas.width, bh = borderStripCanvas.height;
  const ph = panelCanvas.height;
  // Tile the border strip vertically to cover the full panel height in case
  // the panel is taller than the sampled strip (keeps the rope pattern
  // continuous rather than stretching it).
  let y = 0;
  const destX = side === 'left' ? 0 : panelCanvas.width - bw;
  while (y < ph) {
    const sliceH = Math.min(bh, ph - y);
    pctx.drawImage(borderStripCanvas, 0, 0, bw, sliceH, destX, y, bw, sliceH);
    y += sliceH;
  }
}

function extractDielinePanel(img, faceName) {
  // If the person uploaded a dedicated image for this exact face, use it
  // directly — no cropping or crease-detection needed or wanted, since it
  // already IS that face's artwork (e.g. a separate front/back/side/top render).
  if (state.perFaceMode && state.perFaceImgs && state.perFaceImgs[faceName]) {
    return state.perFaceImgs[faceName];
  }
  if (!img) return null;

  const layout = analyzeDielineLayout(img);
  const panel  = layout[faceName];
  if (!panel) return null;

  const c   = document.createElement('canvas');
  c.width   = panel.w;
  c.height  = panel.h;
  const ctx = c.getContext('2d');

  ctx.save();
  if (panel.rotate) {
    ctx.translate(panel.w / 2, panel.h / 2);
    ctx.rotate(Math.PI);
    ctx.translate(-panel.w / 2, -panel.h / 2);
  }
  ctx.drawImage(img, panel.x, panel.y, panel.w, panel.h, 0, 0, panel.w, panel.h);
  ctx.restore();

  // Side panels (front/side/back/other_side) cut from the middle of a
  // continuous wraparound strip have no printed border on their new left/
  // right edges. Stamp a copy of the artwork's own genuine border strip
  // onto those synthetic edges so every panel reads as fully framed,
  // without altering the original border or the source image at all.
  if (!panel.rotate && layout._bodyBox && layout._borderStripCanvas) {
    const bodyBox = layout._bodyBox;
    const strip = layout._borderStripCanvas;
    const isLeftmost  = Math.abs(panel.x - bodyBox.x) < 2;
    const isRightmost = Math.abs((panel.x + panel.w) - (bodyBox.x + bodyBox.w)) < 2;
    if (!isLeftmost)  _stampBorderStrip(c, strip, 'left');
    if (!isRightmost) _stampBorderStrip(c, strip, 'right');
  }

  // Trim empty border rows/columns (white or transparent) that can appear when
  // the body-box boundary detection overshoots, creating white gaps on the 3D face.
  // Only trim body-strip panels (not rotated top panels which have intentional margins).
  if (!panel.rotate) {
    return _trimPanelCanvas(c);
  }

  return c;
}

// ── Panel content trimmer ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// After extracting a panel, trims any empty (background-coloured or transparent)
// border rows/columns so the texture fills the face with no white margins.
// Works on the already-drawn panel canvas — doesn't touch the source image.
function _trimPanelCanvas(panelCanvas) {
  const w = panelCanvas.width, h = panelCanvas.height;
  if (w < 4 || h < 4) return panelCanvas;

  const ctx = panelCanvas.getContext('2d');
  const imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h);
  const data = imgData.data;

  // Sample background colour from canvas corners
  function getRGBA(x, y) {
    const i = (y * w + x) * 4;
    return [data[i], data[i+1], data[i+2], data[i+3]];
  }
  const corners = [getRGBA(0,0), getRGBA(w-1,0), getRGBA(0,h-1), getRGBA(w-1,h-1)];
  let bgR = 0, bgG = 0, bgB = 0, bgA = 0;
  corners.forEach(([r,g,b,a]) => { bgR+=r; bgG+=g; bgB+=b; bgA+=a; });
  bgR/=4; bgG/=4; bgB/=4; bgA/=4;

  const hasAlpha = bgA < 200;
  const THRESH = hasAlpha ? 12 : 22;

  function isContentPixel(x, y) {
    const [r,g,b,a] = getRGBA(x, y);
    if (hasAlpha && Math.abs(a - bgA) > THRESH) return true;
    return Math.sqrt((r-bgR)**2 + (g-bgG)**2 + (b-bgB)**2) > THRESH;
  }

  // Find tight bounds
  let minX = w, maxX = 0, minY = h, maxY = 0;
  for (let y = 0; y < h; y++) {
    for (let x = 0; x < w; x++) {
      if (isContentPixel(x, y)) {
        if (x < minX) minX = x;
        if (x > maxX) maxX = x;
        if (y < minY) minY = y;
        if (y > maxY) maxY = y;
      }
    }
  }

  // If no content found or bounds are nearly the full canvas, skip trim
  if (minX >= maxX || minY >= maxY) return panelCanvas;
  const trimW = maxX - minX + 1, trimH = maxY - minY + 1;
  const marginFracX = minX / w, marginFracY = minY / h;
  // Only trim if the empty margin is > 1% of the panel dimension (avoid over-cropping)
  if (marginFracX < 0.01 && marginFracY < 0.01 &&
      (w - maxX - 1) / w < 0.01 && (h - maxY - 1) / h < 0.01) {
    return panelCanvas; // margins are tiny — no trim needed
  }

  const trimmed = document.createElement('canvas');
  trimmed.width = trimW;
  trimmed.height = trimH;
  trimmed.getContext('2d').drawImage(panelCanvas, minX, minY, trimW, trimH, 0, 0, trimW, trimH);
  return trimmed;
}

/* =========================================================
   COMPOSITING ENGINE — draws design onto scene face
   ========================================================= */

function compositeDesignOnto(ctx, w, h, sceneDrawFn, corners, opacity, blend, customDesignImg, skipBaseDraw){
  if (!skipBaseDraw) {
    sceneDrawFn(ctx, w, h);
  }

  const img = customDesignImg || state.designImg;
  if(!img) return;

  let srcW = img.width, srcH = img.height;
  let sx=0, sy=0;

  const xs = corners.map(p=>p[0]), ys = corners.map(p=>p[1]);
  const bw = Math.max(...xs)-Math.min(...xs);
  const bh = Math.max(...ys)-Math.min(...ys);

  let drawSrcW = srcW, drawSrcH = srcH, cropCanvas = img;
  if(state.fit !== 'stretch'){
    const targetAR = bw/Math.max(bh,0.0001);
    const srcAR = srcW/srcH;
    let cw=srcW, ch=srcH;
    if(state.fit==='cover'){
      if(srcAR > targetAR){ ch = srcH; cw = ch*targetAR; }
      else { cw = srcW; ch = cw/targetAR; }
      sx = (srcW-cw)/2; sy=(srcH-ch)/2;
    } else {
      const off = document.createElement('canvas');
      if(srcAR > targetAR){ off.width = srcW; off.height = srcW/targetAR; }
      else { off.width = srcH*targetAR; off.height = srcH; }
      const octx = off.getContext('2d');
      octx.drawImage(img, (off.width-srcW)/2, (off.height-srcH)/2);
      cropCanvas = off; cw = off.width; ch = off.height; sx=0; sy=0;
    }
    drawSrcW = cw; drawSrcH = ch;
  }

  const prep = document.createElement('canvas');
  prep.width = Math.max(1,drawSrcW); prep.height = Math.max(1,drawSrcH);
  const pctx = prep.getContext('2d');
  pctx.drawImage(cropCanvas, sx, sy, drawSrcW, drawSrcH, 0,0, drawSrcW, drawSrcH);

  // ── Step 1: Warp the design onto the face quad ────────────────────────────
  ctx.save();
  if (state.view === 'top' && state.template.clipTop) {
    state.template.clipTop(ctx, w, h);
  } else if (state.view === 'side' && state.template.clipSide) {
    state.template.clipSide(ctx, w, h);
  } else if (state.view === 'front' && state.template.clipFront) {
    state.template.clipFront(ctx, w, h);
  }
  // Draw design at full opacity first — blend layer applied below
  drawWarpedImage(ctx, prep, prep.width, prep.height, corners);
  ctx.restore();

  // ── Step 2: Blend the base scene texture OVER the design ─────────────────
  // This replicates what multiply/screen blend mode does: the printed surface
  // colour of the box modulates the design, making it look physically wrapped
  // rather than floating on top. Normal mode skips this overlay entirely.
  if (blend !== 'normal') {
    ctx.save();
    // Clip to just this face quad
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...corners[0]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[1]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[2]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[3]);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();
    ctx.globalAlpha = opacity;
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = blend === 'normal' ? 'source-over' : blend;
    const tmp = document.createElement('canvas');
    tmp.width=w; tmp.height=h;
    sceneDrawFn(tmp.getContext('2d'), w, h);
    ctx.drawImage(tmp,0,0);
    ctx.restore();
  }

  // ── Step 3: Specular & edge shading for wrap realism ─────────────────────
  if (state.template && state.template.rig) {
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...corners[0]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[1]);
    ctx.lineTo(...corners[2]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[3]);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();

    const minX = Math.min(...xs), maxX = Math.max(...xs);
    const minY = Math.min(...ys), maxY = Math.max(...ys);

    // Determine light direction based on view face
    const view = state.view;
    let grad;
    if (view === 'top') {
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(minX, minY, maxX, maxY);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(255,255,255,0.14)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.45,'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)');
    } else if (view === 'side' || view === 'other_side') {
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(minX, minY, maxX, minY);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.10)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.04)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.16)');
    } else {
      // front / back — key light from upper-left
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(minX, minY, maxX, maxY);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(255,255,255,0.09)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.4, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.7, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.01)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.09)');
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();

    // Edge crease — thin dark outline per face
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.20)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(...corners[0]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[1]);
    ctx.lineTo(...corners[2]); ctx.lineTo(...corners[3]);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();
  }
}

/* =========================================================
   RENDER STAGE
   ========================================================= */

function renderStage(){
  const tpl = state.template;
  const [w,h] = tpl.canvas;
  stageCanvas.width = w; stageCanvas.height = h;
  overlayCanvas.width = w; overlayCanvas.height = h;
  stageCanvas.style.width = overlayCanvas.style.width = '100%';
  stageCanvas.style.height = overlayCanvas.style.height = 'auto';

  const threeCanvas = document.getElementById('threeCanvas');
  const is3DActive = (state.view==='3d' && tpl.turntable);
  
  if (is3DActive) {
    if (threeCanvas) threeCanvas.style.display = 'block';
    stageCanvas.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    overlayCanvas.style.display = 'none';
  } else {
    if (threeCanvas) threeCanvas.style.display = 'none';
    stageCanvas.style.visibility = 'visible';
    overlayCanvas.style.display = 'block';
  }

  if(is3DActive){
    renderStage360();
    return;
  }

  // Resolve drawing function for custom view
  let drawFn = tpl.draw;
  if(state.view === 'front' && tpl.drawFront) drawFn = tpl.drawFront;
  else if(state.view === 'side' && tpl.drawSide) drawFn = tpl.drawSide;
  else if(state.view === 'back' && tpl.drawBack) drawFn = tpl.drawBack;
  else if(state.view === 'back' && tpl.drawFront) drawFn = tpl.drawFront;
  else if(state.view === 'other_side' && tpl.drawOtherSide) drawFn = tpl.drawOtherSide;
  else if(state.view === 'other_side' && tpl.drawSide) drawFn = tpl.drawSide;
  else if(state.view === 'top' && tpl.drawTop) drawFn = tpl.drawTop;

  // base scene
  const quads = drawFn(stageCtx, w, h);

  if(state.designImg){
    canvasFrame.style.display='block';
    emptyState.style.display='none';
    
    if (state.view === '3d' && state.dielineMode && quads) {
      Object.keys(quads).forEach(faceName => {
        const designPanel = extractDielinePanel(state.designImg, faceName);
        if (designPanel) {
          compositeDesignOnto(stageCtx, w, h, drawFn, quads[faceName], state.opacity, state.blend, designPanel, true);
        }
      });
    } else {
      let designToUse = state.designImg;
      if (state.dielineMode) {
        designToUse = extractDielinePanel(state.designImg, state.view) || state.designImg;
      }
      compositeDesignOnto(stageCtx, w, h, drawFn, state.corners, state.opacity, state.blend, designToUse, true);
    }
  } else {
    // Always show the template preview even without a design loaded
    canvasFrame.style.display = 'block';
    emptyState.style.display = 'none';
  }

  drawOverlayPins();
  updateFooter();
  exportBtn.disabled = !state.designImg;
}

function renderStage360(){
  initThree();
  
  const tpl = state.template;
  const [w,h] = tpl.canvas;
  
  canvasFrame.style.display='block';
  emptyState.style.display='none';
  
  // Set dimensions
  const threeCanvas = document.getElementById('threeCanvas');
  threeCanvas.width = w;
  threeCanvas.height = h;
  threeRenderer.setSize(w, h, false);
  threeCamera.aspect = w / h;
  threeCamera.updateProjectionMatrix();
  
  // Rebuild/update materials and meshes if parameters changed
  const designSrc = state.designImg ? state.designImg.src : null;
  const needsRebuild = (
    threeCache.templateId !== tpl.id ||
    threeCache.designSrc !== designSrc ||
    threeCache.opacity !== state.opacity ||
    threeCache.blend !== state.blend ||
    threeCache.fit !== state.fit ||
    threeCache.dielineMode !== state.dielineMode
  );
  
  if (needsRebuild) {
    updateThreeModel();
    threeCache = {
      templateId: tpl.id,
      designSrc: designSrc,
      opacity: state.opacity,
      blend: state.blend,
      fit: state.fit,
      dielineMode: state.dielineMode
    };
  }
  
  // Sync camera position with state.ttAngle (preventing feedback loop).
  // Also set a template-appropriate Y elevation so each shape type is
  // framed well: tube boxes are flat/wide so camera should be near mid-height;
  // cans and bottles are tall so a slight elevation looks natural.
  isUpdatingCamera = true;
  const radius = Math.sqrt(threeCamera.position.x**2 + threeCamera.position.z**2) || 10;
  const angleRad = state.ttAngle * Math.PI / 180;
  threeCamera.position.x = radius * Math.sin(angleRad);
  threeCamera.position.z = radius * Math.cos(angleRad);
  const isTube = tpl.rig === 'box' && tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.tube;
  const isSachet = tpl.rig === 'sachet';
  threeCamera.position.y = isTube ? 0.5 : (isSachet ? 0 : 1.5);
  threeCamera.lookAt(0, 0, 0);
  threeControls.update();
  isUpdatingCamera = false;
  
  // WebGL Render
  threeRenderer.render(threeScene, threeCamera);
  
  updateFooter();
  exportBtn.disabled = !state.designImg;
}


function drawOverlayPins(){
