  overlayCtx.clearRect(0,0,overlayCanvas.width, overlayCanvas.height);
  if(!state.pinsVisible) return;
  const pts = state.corners;
  overlayCtx.save();
  overlayCtx.strokeStyle = '#FF5A1F';
  overlayCtx.lineWidth = 2.5;
  overlayCtx.setLineDash([6,5]);
  overlayCtx.beginPath();
  pts.forEach((p,i)=>i===0?overlayCtx.moveTo(p[0],p[1]):overlayCtx.lineTo(p[0],p[1]));
  overlayCtx.closePath();
  overlayCtx.stroke();
  overlayCtx.setLineDash([]);

  pts.forEach((p,i)=>{
    overlayCtx.beginPath();
    overlayCtx.arc(p[0],p[1], 12, 0, Math.PI*2);
    overlayCtx.fillStyle = '#0E0E10';
    overlayCtx.fill();
    overlayCtx.lineWidth = 2.5;
    overlayCtx.strokeStyle = '#FF5A1F';
    overlayCtx.stroke();
    overlayCtx.fillStyle = '#FF5A1F';
    overlayCtx.font = '600 13px JetBrains Mono, monospace';
    overlayCtx.textAlign='center';
    overlayCtx.textBaseline='middle';
    overlayCtx.fillText(String(i+1), p[0], p[1]);
  });
  overlayCtx.restore();
}

function updateFooter(){
  if(state.view==='3d' && state.template.turntable){
    const status = state.designImg ? 'turntable composited' : 'turntable preview';
    footerStatus.textContent = `${status} · ${state.template.canvas[0]}×${state.template.canvas[1]}px · ${state.blend} · ${Math.round(state.ttAngle)}°`;
    cornerCoords.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  if(!state.designImg){
    footerStatus.textContent = 'awaiting template + design';
  } else {
    footerStatus.textContent = `composited · ${state.template.canvas[0]}×${state.template.canvas[1]}px · ${state.blend}`;
  }
  cornerCoords.innerHTML = state.corners.map((p,i)=>
    `<span>c${i+1} <b>${Math.round(p[0])},${Math.round(p[1])}</b></span>`
  ).join('');
}

/* =========================================================
   PIN DRAGGING
   ========================================================= */
function canvasPointFromEvent(e){
  const rect = overlayCanvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  const scaleX = overlayCanvas.width/rect.width;
  const scaleY = overlayCanvas.height/rect.height;
  const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
  const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
  return [(clientX-rect.left)*scaleX, (clientY-rect.top)*scaleY];
}

overlayCanvas.addEventListener('mousedown', e=>{
  if(!state.pinsVisible) return;
  const [x,y] = canvasPointFromEvent(e);
  let closest=-1, minD=26;
  state.corners.forEach((p,i)=>{
    const d = Math.hypot(p[0]-x, p[1]-y);
    if(d<minD){ minD=d; closest=i; }
  });
  if(closest>=0){ state.dragIdx = closest; overlayCanvas.style.cursor='grabbing'; }
});
window.addEventListener('mousemove', e=>{
  if(state.dragIdx<0) return;
  const [x,y] = canvasPointFromEvent(e);
  state.corners[state.dragIdx] = [
    Math.max(0,Math.min(state.template.canvas[0],x)),
    Math.max(0,Math.min(state.template.canvas[1],y))
  ];
  const key = state.template.id + '_' + state.view;
  state.customCorners[key] = state.corners.map(p=>p.slice());
  renderStage();
});
window.addEventListener('mouseup', ()=>{
  if(state.dragIdx>=0){ state.dragIdx=-1; overlayCanvas.style.cursor='default'; }
});
overlayCanvas.addEventListener('mousemove', e=>{
  if(!state.pinsVisible || state.dragIdx>=0) return;
  const [x,y] = canvasPointFromEvent(e);
  const near = state.corners.some(p=>Math.hypot(p[0]-x,p[1]-y)<26);
  overlayCanvas.style.cursor = near ? 'grab' : 'default';
});

pinToggle.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  state.pinsVisible = !state.pinsVisible;
  pinToggle.classList.toggle('on', state.pinsVisible);
  pinToggleLabel.textContent = state.pinsVisible ? 'hide corner pins' : 'show corner pins';
  renderStage();
});

resetBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  const key = state.template.id + '_' + state.view;
  delete state.customCorners[key];
  updateCornersForView();
  renderStage();
  showToast('Corner pins reset');
});

/* =========================================================
   FILE UPLOAD
   ========================================================= */
const ACCEPTED_DESIGN_TYPES = /image\/(png|jpe?g|svg\+xml)|application\/pdf/;
const ACCEPTED_DESIGN_EXT = /\.(png|jpe?g|svg|pdf)$/i;

function loadDesignFromImageSrc(src, file){
  const img = new Image();
  img.onload = ()=>{
    state.designImg = img;
    state.designName = file.name;
    _dielineCache = { src: null, tplId: null, layout: null };
    renderFileChip();
    if (state.dielineMode) renderDielinePreview();
    // Auto-fit template dimensions to detected design aspect ratio
    if (typeof matchAspectRatio === 'function') matchAspectRatio();
    renderStage();
    showToast('Design loaded');
  };
  img.onerror = ()=>{
    showToast('Could not read that file', true);
  };
  img.src = src;
}

async function loadDesignFromPdf(file){
  if(typeof pdfjsLib === 'undefined'){
    showToast('PDF support failed to load', true);
    return;
  }
  try{
    pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.min.js';
    const buf = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: buf }).promise;
    const page = await pdf.getPage(1);

    // Render at a high scale so the rasterized design stays crisp on the mockup.
    const targetScale = Math.min(4, 2400 / Math.max(page.getViewport({ scale: 1 }).width, page.getViewport({ scale: 1 }).height));
    const viewport = page.getViewport({ scale: Math.max(2, targetScale) });

    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.width = Math.ceil(viewport.width);
    canvas.height = Math.ceil(viewport.height);
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    // White backdrop so transparent PDF regions don't render black on the mockup.
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    await page.render({ canvasContext: ctx, viewport }).promise;
    loadDesignFromImageSrc(canvas.toDataURL('image/png'), file);
  }catch(err){
    console.error(err);
    showToast('Could not read that PDF', true);
  }
}

function handleFile(file){
  if(!file || !(ACCEPTED_DESIGN_TYPES.test(file.type) || ACCEPTED_DESIGN_EXT.test(file.name))){
    showToast('PNG, JPG, SVG, or PDF only', true);
    return;
  }

  const isPdf = file.type === 'application/pdf' || /\.pdf$/i.test(file.name);
  if(isPdf){
    loadDesignFromPdf(file);
    return;
  }

  // PNG, JPG/JPEG, and SVG can all be loaded directly as an <img> source.
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = ev=> loadDesignFromImageSrc(ev.target.result, file);
  reader.onerror = ()=> showToast('Could not read that file', true);
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
}

function renderFileChip(){
  fileChipHolder.innerHTML = '';
  const metaInfo = document.getElementById('designMetaInfo');
  
  if(!state.designImg) {
    if (metaInfo) {
      metaInfo.style.display = 'none';
      metaInfo.innerHTML = '';
    }
    return;
  }
  
  const chip = document.createElement('div');
  chip.className = 'file-chip';
  chip.innerHTML = `
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="1.5"/><path d="M21 15l-5-5L5 21"/></svg>
    <span class="name">${state.designName}</span>
    <span class="clear" title="Remove">&times;</span>
  `;
  chip.querySelector('.clear').addEventListener('click', ()=>{
    state.designImg = null; state.designName='';
    fileChipHolder.innerHTML='';
    if (metaInfo) {
      metaInfo.style.display = 'none';
      metaInfo.innerHTML = '';
    }
    renderStage();
  });
  fileChipHolder.appendChild(chip);

  if (metaInfo) {
    const w = state.designImg.naturalWidth || state.designImg.width;
    const h = state.designImg.naturalHeight || state.designImg.height;
    if (w && h) {
      const ar = w / h;
      metaInfo.style.display = 'block';
      metaInfo.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; background:#161618; border:1px solid var(--line); border-radius:6px; padding:6px 10px; margin-top:8px; gap:8px;">
          <div style="font-family:var(--mono); font-size:10px; color:var(--slate-dark);">
            <span style="color:var(--slate);">Dims:</span> <b>${w}&times;${h}</b> <span style="color:var(--slate);">(${ar.toFixed(2)}:1)</span>
          </div>
          <button id="matchRatioBtn" type="button" style="padding:4px 8px; background:var(--signal); border:none; border-radius:4px; color:#fff; font-family:var(--sans); font-size:9.5px; font-weight:700; cursor:pointer; transition:opacity .15s;">
            MATCH RATIO
          </button>
        </div>
      `;
      document.getElementById('matchRatioBtn').addEventListener('click', matchAspectRatio);
    } else {
      metaInfo.style.display = 'none';
      metaInfo.innerHTML = '';
    }
  }
}

dropzone.addEventListener('click', ()=>fileInput.click());
fileInput.addEventListener('change', e=> handleFile(e.target.files[0]));
['dragenter','dragover'].forEach(evt=>{
  dropzone.addEventListener(evt, e=>{ e.preventDefault(); dropzone.classList.add('drag'); });
});
['dragleave','drop'].forEach(evt=>{
  dropzone.addEventListener(evt, e=>{ e.preventDefault(); dropzone.classList.remove('drag'); });
});
dropzone.addEventListener('drop', e=>{
  const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
  handleFile(file);
});

/* =========================================================
   CONTROLS
   ========================================================= */
blendSeg.addEventListener('click', e=>{
  const btn = e.target.closest('button'); if(!btn) return;
  [...blendSeg.children].forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  state.blend = btn.dataset.mode;
  metaBlend.textContent = state.blend;
  renderStage();
});

fitSeg.addEventListener('click', e=>{
  const btn = e.target.closest('button'); if(!btn) return;
  [...fitSeg.children].forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  btn.classList.add('active');
  state.fit = btn.dataset.fit;
  fitVal.textContent = state.fit;
  renderStage();
});

opacitySlider.addEventListener('input', e=>{
  state.opacity = e.target.value/100;
  opacityVal.textContent = e.target.value+'%';
  renderStage();
});

dielineModeCheckbox.addEventListener('change', e=>{
  state.dielineMode = e.target.checked;
  const previewSection = document.getElementById('dielinePreviewSection');
  previewSection.style.display = (state.dielineMode && !state.perFaceMode) ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (state.dielineMode && state.designImg) {
    renderDielinePreview();
  }
  renderStage();
});

// ── Per-face separate image upload ──────────────────────────────────────────
// For designs that were never a single flat dieline in the first place (e.g. a
// set of individually rendered/photographed front, back, side, and top shots),
// asking the auto-detector to slice one image into five fake regions can never
// be correct — the other faces' real artwork simply isn't present in that one
// image. This mode sidesteps detection entirely: each face gets its own
// uploaded image, applied 1:1, guaranteed correct regardless of source layout.
const PER_FACE_LIST = [
  { key: 'front',      label: 'Front' },
  { key: 'side',       label: 'Side' },
  { key: 'back',       label: 'Back' },
  { key: 'other_side', label: 'Other Side' },
  { key: 'top',        label: 'Top' }
];

(function initPerFaceGrid() {
  const grid = document.getElementById('perFaceGrid');
  const perFaceModeCheckbox = document.getElementById('perFaceModeCheckbox');
  if (!grid || !perFaceModeCheckbox) return;

  PER_FACE_LIST.forEach(({ key, label }) => {
    const cell = document.createElement('div');
    cell.style.cssText = 'border:1.5px dashed var(--line-soft); border-radius:6px; padding:8px; text-align:center; cursor:pointer; transition:all .15s ease; background:rgba(255,255,255,.015); position:relative; min-height:64px; display:flex; flex-direction:column; align-items:center; justify-content:center; gap:4px;';
    cell.innerHTML = `
      <input type="file" accept="image/png,image/jpeg,image/jpg,image/webp" style="display:none;" id="perFaceInput_${key}">
      <img id="perFaceThumb_${key}" style="display:none; max-width:100%; max-height:36px; border-radius:3px; object-fit:contain;">
      <span id="perFaceLabel_${key}" style="font-family:var(--mono); font-size:9.5px; color:var(--slate-dark);">${label}</span>
      <span id="perFaceClear_${key}" style="display:none; position:absolute; top:2px; right:4px; font-size:11px; color:var(--slate); cursor:pointer;">×</span>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(cell);

    const input = cell.querySelector(`#perFaceInput_${key}`);
    const thumb = cell.querySelector(`#perFaceThumb_${key}`);
    const labelEl = cell.querySelector(`#perFaceLabel_${key}`);
    const clearBtn = cell.querySelector(`#perFaceClear_${key}`);

    cell.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target !== clearBtn) input.click(); });
    cell.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); cell.style.borderColor = 'var(--signal)'; });
    cell.addEventListener('dragleave', () => { cell.style.borderColor = 'var(--line-soft)'; });
    cell.addEventListener('drop', e => {
      e.preventDefault();
      cell.style.borderColor = 'var(--line-soft)';
      const f = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
      if (f) loadPerFaceFile(f);
    });
    input.addEventListener('change', () => { if (input.files[0]) loadPerFaceFile(input.files[0]); });
    clearBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      state.perFaceImgs[key] = null;
      thumb.style.display = 'none';
      labelEl.style.display = 'block';
      clearBtn.style.display = 'none';
      input.value = '';
      renderStage();
    });

    function loadPerFaceFile(file) {
      if (!file || !file.type.startsWith('image/')) return;
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = e => {
        const img = new Image();
        img.onload = () => {
          state.perFaceImgs[key] = img;
          thumb.src = e.target.result;
          thumb.style.display = 'block';
          labelEl.style.display = 'none';
          clearBtn.style.display = 'block';
          // Satisfy the "something is uploaded" gate that drives rendering,
          // in case the person hasn't also filled the main design dropzone.
          if (!state.designImg) { state.designImg = img; state.designName = file.name; }
          renderStage();
        };
        img.src = e.target.result;
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    }
  });

  perFaceModeCheckbox.addEventListener('change', e => {
    state.perFaceMode = e.target.checked;
    grid.style.display = state.perFaceMode ? 'grid' : 'none';
    const previewSection = document.getElementById('dielinePreviewSection');
    if (state.perFaceMode) {
      // Per-face mode needs the "apply per quad face" render branch, which is
      // gated on dielineMode — force it on and lock the checkbox while active.
      dielineModeCheckbox.checked = true;
      state.dielineMode = true;
      dielineModeCheckbox.disabled = true;
      if (previewSection) previewSection.style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      dielineModeCheckbox.disabled = false;
      if (previewSection) previewSection.style.display = state.dielineMode ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (state.dielineMode && state.designImg) renderDielinePreview();
    }
    renderStage();
  });
})();

const FACE_COLORS = {
  top:        'rgba(255,200,50,0.35)',
  front:      'rgba(61,220,151,0.35)',
  side:       'rgba(100,149,237,0.35)',
  back:       'rgba(255,90,31,0.35)',
  other_side: 'rgba(200,100,255,0.35)'
};
const FACE_LABELS = {
  top: 'TOP', front: 'FRONT', side: 'SIDE', back: 'BACK', other_side: 'OTHER SIDE'
};

function renderDielinePreview() {
  const img = state.designImg;
  if (!img) return;

  const layout = analyzeDielineLayout(img);
  const previewCanvas = document.getElementById('dielinePreviewCanvas');
  const countEl = document.getElementById('dielinePanelCount');
  const legendEl = document.getElementById('dielinePanelLegend');

  const previewW = 230;
  const sc = previewW / img.width;
  const previewH = Math.round(img.height * sc);
  previewCanvas.width = previewW;
  previewCanvas.height = previewH;
  const ctx = previewCanvas.getContext('2d');

  // Draw the image with a subtle chequered bg to show transparency
  const patSize = 8;
  for (let py = 0; py < previewH; py += patSize) {
    for (let px = 0; px < previewW; px += patSize) {
      ctx.fillStyle = ((Math.floor(px/patSize)+Math.floor(py/patSize))%2===0) ? '#2a2a2e' : '#1c1c1f';
      ctx.fillRect(px, py, patSize, patSize);
    }
  }
  ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, previewW, previewH);

  // Only count real faces (skip private keys starting with _)
  const faceNames = Object.keys(layout).filter(k => !k.startsWith('_'));
  countEl.textContent = faceNames.length + ' faces detected';
  legendEl.innerHTML = '';

  // Draw detected gap lines (crease detection result) with drag handles
  _dielinePreviewGeom = { sc, previewW, previewH, splitXs: [], topBoundaryY: null, bodyBox: layout._bodyBox };
  if (layout._splitXs && layout._splitXs.length > 0) {
    ctx.save();
    ctx.setLineDash([3, 2]);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.45)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    layout._splitXs.forEach(gx => {
      const px = gx * sc;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(px, 0);
      ctx.lineTo(px, previewH);
      ctx.stroke();
    });
    ctx.restore();
    _dielinePreviewGeom.splitXs = layout._splitXs.slice();

    // Grip handles (small pill shapes) at mid-height so it's obvious these are draggable
    layout._splitXs.forEach(gx => {
      const px = gx * sc, py = previewH / 2;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,20,22,0.9)';
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.roundRect(px - 6, py - 12, 12, 24, 4); ctx.fill();
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.8)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px - 2, py - 7); ctx.lineTo(px - 2, py + 7); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px + 2, py - 7); ctx.lineTo(px + 2, py + 7); ctx.stroke();
    });
  }

  // Draggable top/body boundary (horizontal line) if a top panel exists
  if (layout.top) {
    const boundaryY = (layout._bodyBox ? layout._bodyBox.y : (layout.top.y + layout.top.h)) * sc;
    _dielinePreviewGeom.topBoundaryY = layout._bodyBox ? layout._bodyBox.y : (layout.top.y + layout.top.h);
    ctx.save();
    ctx.setLineDash([3, 2]);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,200,50,0.7)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, boundaryY); ctx.lineTo(previewW, boundaryY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();
    const hx = previewW / 2;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,20,22,0.9)';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.roundRect(hx - 12, boundaryY - 6, 24, 12, 4); ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,200,50,0.9)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(hx - 7, boundaryY - 2); ctx.lineTo(hx + 7, boundaryY - 2); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(hx - 7, boundaryY + 2); ctx.lineTo(hx + 7, boundaryY + 2); ctx.stroke();
  }

  faceNames.forEach(name => {
    const p = layout[name];
    if (!p || p.w <= 0 || p.h <= 0) return;

    const x = p.x * sc, y = p.y * sc, w = p.w * sc, h = p.h * sc;
    const color = FACE_COLORS[name] || 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)';
    const solidColor = color.replace(/[\d.]+\)$/, '0.9)');

    // Fill panel zone
    ctx.fillStyle = color;
    ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, h);

    // Panel border
    ctx.strokeStyle = solidColor;
    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    ctx.strokeRect(x + 0.75, y + 0.75, w - 1.5, h - 1.5);

    // Dashed dividers for inner panels
    if (name !== 'top') {
      ctx.save();
      ctx.setLineDash([3, 3]);
      ctx.strokeStyle = solidColor;
      ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      ctx.strokeRect(x + 0.75, y + 0.75, w - 1.5, h - 1.5);
      ctx.restore();
    }

    const label = FACE_LABELS[name] || name.toUpperCase();
    ctx.font = '700 9px JetBrains Mono, monospace';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';

    const metrics = ctx.measureText(label);
    const lw = metrics.width + 10, lh = 14;
    const lx = x + w / 2, ly = y + h / 2;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(10,10,12,0.82)';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.roundRect(lx - lw/2, ly - lh/2, lw, lh, 3);
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.fillStyle = solidColor;
    ctx.fillText(label, lx, ly);

    const dot = document.createElement('span');
    dot.style.cssText = `display:inline-flex; align-items:center; gap:4px; color:var(--slate-dark); font-size:9.5px;`;
    dot.innerHTML = `<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:2px;background:${solidColor};display:inline-block;flex-shrink:0;"></span>${label}`;
    legendEl.appendChild(dot);
  });

  // Badge: detection method used
  const methodBadge = document.createElement('span');
  const autoGap = layout._detectedGaps && layout._splitXs &&
    layout._detectedGaps.length > 0 &&
    layout._detectedGaps.length === layout._splitXs.length;
  const edgeDetected = layout._edgeDetected;
  let badgeText, badgeColor;
  if (layout._manualOverride) {
    badgeText = '✎ manually adjusted';
    badgeColor = 'var(--signal)';
  } else if (autoGap) {
    badgeText = '✓ crease-line auto-detected';
    badgeColor = 'var(--go)';
  } else if (edgeDetected) {
    badgeText = '✓ color-edge detection used';
    badgeColor = 'var(--go)';
  } else {
    badgeText = '~ ratio-based split (no gap found) — drag the lines above to fix';
    badgeColor = 'var(--slate)';
  }
  methodBadge.style.cssText = `display:block; width:100%; margin-top:4px; font-size:8.5px; font-family:var(--mono); color:${badgeColor};`;
  methodBadge.textContent = badgeText;
  legendEl.appendChild(methodBadge);

  const resetBtn = document.getElementById('dielineResetBtn');
  if (resetBtn) resetBtn.style.display = layout._manualOverride ? 'block' : 'none';
}

// ── Manual drag-to-fix editing of the Detected Panels preview ──────────────
// Geometry of the last render, so drag handlers can hit-test in preview
// (canvas) pixel space and convert back to full-resolution image pixel space.
let _dielinePreviewGeom = { sc: 1, previewW: 0, previewH: 0, splitXs: [], topBoundaryY: null, bodyBox: null };
let _dielineDrag = null; // { type: 'split'|'top', index?: number }

function _seedManualOverrideFromCurrentLayout(img) {
  if (_manualDielineOverride && _manualDielineOverride.srcKey === img.src) return _manualDielineOverride;
  const layout = analyzeDielineLayout(img);
  _manualDielineOverride = {
    srcKey: img.src,
    bodyBox: layout._bodyBox ? { ...layout._bodyBox } : null,
    splitXs: layout._splitXs ? layout._splitXs.slice() : [],
    topBox: layout.top ? { x: layout.top.x, y: layout.top.y, w: layout.top.w, h: layout.top.h } : null
  };
  return _manualDielineOverride;
}

function _dielineHandleAt(mx, my) {
  const g = _dielinePreviewGeom;
  const HIT = 10;
  if (g.topBoundaryY !== null) {
    const by = g.topBoundaryY * g.sc;
    if (Math.abs(my - by) <= HIT && Math.abs(mx - g.previewW / 2) <= 14) return { type: 'top' };
  }
  for (let i = 0; i < g.splitXs.length; i++) {
    const px = g.splitXs[i] * g.sc;
    if (Math.abs(mx - px) <= HIT) return { type: 'split', index: i };
  }
  return null;
}

(function initDielineDragHandlers() {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('dielinePreviewCanvas');
  const resetBtn = document.getElementById('dielineResetBtn');
  if (!canvas) return;

  function getPos(e) {
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const scX = canvas.width / rect.width, scY = canvas.height / rect.height;
    const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
    const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
    return { x: (clientX - rect.left) * scX, y: (clientY - rect.top) * scY };
  }

  function onDown(e) {
    if (!state.designImg) return;
    const pos = getPos(e);
    const hit = _dielineHandleAt(pos.x, pos.y);
    if (!hit) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    _seedManualOverrideFromCurrentLayout(state.designImg);
    _dielineDrag = hit;
  }

  function onMove(e) {
    if (!_dielineDrag || !state.designImg) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    const pos = getPos(e);
    const g = _dielinePreviewGeom;
    const imgX = pos.x / g.sc, imgY = pos.y / g.sc;
    const ov = _manualDielineOverride;
    if (!ov) return;

    if (_dielineDrag.type === 'split') {
      const i = _dielineDrag.index;
      const bodyBox = ov.bodyBox || { x: 0, w: state.designImg.width };
      const lo = i === 0 ? bodyBox.x + 4 : ov.splitXs[i - 1] + 4;
      const hi = i === ov.splitXs.length - 1 ? bodyBox.x + bodyBox.w - 4 : ov.splitXs[i + 1] - 4;
      ov.splitXs[i] = Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, Math.round(imgX)));
    } else if (_dielineDrag.type === 'top') {
      const bodyBox = ov.bodyBox;
      if (!bodyBox || !ov.topBox) return;
      const minY = ov.topBox.y + 8;
      const maxY = bodyBox.y + bodyBox.h - 8;
      const newBoundaryY = Math.max(minY, Math.min(maxY, Math.round(imgY)));
      const bottomY = bodyBox.y + bodyBox.h;
      ov.topBox.h = newBoundaryY - ov.topBox.y;
      bodyBox.y = newBoundaryY;
      bodyBox.h = bottomY - newBoundaryY;
    }

    _dielineCache = { src: null, tplId: null, layout: null }; // invalidate memoized layout
    renderDielinePreview();
    renderStage();
  }

  function onUp() { _dielineDrag = null; }

  canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', onDown);
  window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
  window.addEventListener('mouseup', onUp);
  canvas.addEventListener('touchstart', onDown, { passive: false });
  window.addEventListener('touchmove', onMove, { passive: false });
  window.addEventListener('touchend', onUp);

  if (resetBtn) {
    resetBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      _manualDielineOverride = null;
      _dielineCache = { src: null, tplId: null, layout: null };
      if (state.designImg) { renderDielinePreview(); renderStage(); }
    });
  }
})();

/* =========================================================
   EXPORT
   ========================================================= */
exportBtn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  if(!state.designImg) return;
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  const is3D = (state.view==='3d' && state.template.turntable);
  if(is3D){
    link.download = `mockup-${state.template.id}-${Math.round(state.ttAngle)}deg.png`;
    const threeCanvas = document.getElementById('threeCanvas');
    link.href = threeCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
  } else {
    link.download = `mockup-${state.template.id}-${state.view}.png`;
    link.href = stageCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
  }
  link.click();
  showToast('Exported PNG');
});

frameSeqBtn.addEventListener('click', async ()=>{
  if(!state.designImg || !state.template.turntable) return;
  setView('3d');
  stopTurntableSpin();
  const wasAngle = state.ttAngle;
  const steps = 12;
  frameSeqBtn.disabled = true;
  for(let i=0;i<steps;i++){
    const ang = Math.round(i*(360/steps));
    state.ttAngle = ang;
    ttSlider.value = ang;
    ttDeg.textContent = ang + '\u00B0';
    renderStage();
    await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,0));
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.download = `mockup-${state.template.id}-${String(ang).padStart(3,'0')}deg.png`;
    const threeCanvas = document.getElementById('threeCanvas');
    link.href = threeCanvas.toDataURL('image/png');
    link.click();
    await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,120));
  }
  state.ttAngle = wasAngle;
  ttSlider.value = wasAngle;
  ttDeg.textContent = Math.round(wasAngle) + '\u00B0';
  renderStage();
  frameSeqBtn.disabled = false;
  showToast('Exported 12-frame turntable set');
});

/* =========================================================
   TOAST
   ========================================================= */
let toastTimer;
function showToast(msg, isErr){
  toastMsg.textContent = msg;
  toast.querySelector('.dot').style.background = isErr ? '#FF5A1F' : '#3DDC97';
  toast.classList.add('show');
  clearTimeout(toastTimer);
  toastTimer = setTimeout(()=>toast.classList.remove('show'), 2200);
}


/* =========================================================
   THREE.JS 3D ENGINE
   ========================================================= */
let threeScene, threeCamera, threeRenderer, threeControls;
let threeMesh = null;
let isUpdatingCamera = false;
let threeCache = {
  templateId: null,
  designSrc: null,
  opacity: null,
  blend: null,
  fit: null,
  dielineMode: null
};

function drawBasePaperTexture(ctx, w, h, baseColor) {
  ctx.fillStyle = baseColor;
  ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);
  
  // Subtle paper grain noise
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.025)';
  const numDots = Math.round((w * h) / 1300);
  for (let i = 0; i < numDots; i++) {
    const rx = Math.random() * w;
    const ry = Math.random() * h;
    ctx.fillRect(rx, ry, Math.random() * 2 + 1, Math.random() * 2 + 1);
  }
  
  // Vertical fibers/lines
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.015)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  const lineSpacing = w > 1000 ? 16 : 6;
  for (let i = 0; i < w; i += lineSpacing) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(i, 0);
    ctx.lineTo(i, h);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
}

function createFaceTextureCanvas(faceName, tpl) {
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  let tw = 2048, th = 2048;
  
  // Extract the dieline panel first so we know its EXACT pixel dimensions.
  // The texture canvas must match those dimensions exactly — otherwise Three.js
  // will stretch the texture to fill the UV space and the image will be distorted.
  let dielinePanel = null;
  if (state.dielineMode && state.designImg) {
    dielinePanel = extractDielinePanel(state.designImg, faceName);
    if (dielinePanel && dielinePanel.width > 0 && dielinePanel.height > 0) {
      // Use exact panel pixel size (capped at 4096 for GPU safety).
      // NO aspect-ratio math — we use the raw dimensions so the texture
      // fills the UV quad with 1:1 pixel correspondence and zero stretching.
      const MAX_TEX = 4096;
      const scaleDown = Math.min(1, MAX_TEX / Math.max(dielinePanel.width, dielinePanel.height));
      tw = Math.max(4, Math.round(dielinePanel.width  * scaleDown));
      th = Math.max(4, Math.round(dielinePanel.height * scaleDown));
    }
  }
  
  // For non-dieline mode, use fixed proportions based on box geometry
  if (!state.dielineMode || !dielinePanel) {
    if (tpl.rig === 'box') {
      const square = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.square);
      const tube = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.tube);
      if (faceName === 'front' || faceName === 'back') {
        tw = 2048; th = tube ? 500 : (square ? 2048 : 1880);
      } else if (faceName === 'side' || faceName === 'other_side') {
        tw = tube ? 190 : (square ? 2048 : 1000); th = tube ? 500 : (square ? 2048 : 1880);
      } else if (faceName === 'top') {
        tw = 2048; th = tube ? 190 : (square ? 2048 : 1000);
      }
    } else if (tpl.rig === 'sachet') {
      tw = 2048; th = 4096;
    }
  }

  // Swap canvas dimensions for top face to match rotated orientation mapped by Three.js.
  // In dieline mode tw/th are the panel's real pixel dims — NO swap needed there.
  // The drawImage rotation inside the draw block handles orientation mapping instead.
  if (faceName === 'top' && !(state.dielineMode && dielinePanel)) {
    const temp = tw;
    tw = th;
    th = temp;
  }
  
  canvas.width = tw;
  canvas.height = th;
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  
  if (tpl.rig === 'box') {
    let baseColor = '#DCD5C2';
    if (faceName === 'side' || faceName === 'other_side') baseColor = '#B8AD95';
    if (faceName === 'top') baseColor = '#EDE9DD';
    drawBasePaperTexture(ctx, tw, th, baseColor);
  } else if (tpl.rig === 'sachet') {
    ctx.fillStyle = '#f2efe6';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
    
    // Draw sachet metallic crimped seals
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, 160);
    ctx.fillRect(0, th - 160, tw, 160);
    
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 4;
    for (let i = 16; i < 160; i += 24) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, i); ctx.lineTo(tw, i); ctx.stroke();
    }
    for (let i = th - 144; i < th; i += 24) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, i); ctx.lineTo(tw, i); ctx.stroke();
    }
  } else if (tpl.rig === 'tin') {
    // Silver metallic base
    const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
    grad.addColorStop(0,    '#7a8090');
    grad.addColorStop(0.12, '#c8cdd8');
    grad.addColorStop(0.40, '#e8eaf0');
    grad.addColorStop(0.55, '#f5f6fa');
    grad.addColorStop(0.72, '#d0d4de');
    grad.addColorStop(0.88, '#9aa0ae');
    grad.addColorStop(1,    '#6a7080');
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
  } else if (tpl.rig === 'bottle') {
    // Glass green base — use opaque base fill first so the canvas has no alpha-transparent pixels
    ctx.fillStyle = '#a8c4a0';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
    const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
    grad.addColorStop(0,   '#506456');
    grad.addColorStop(0.20,'#82a591');
    grad.addColorStop(0.45,'#c8e6d2');
    grad.addColorStop(0.55,'#e6faeb');
    grad.addColorStop(0.75,'#a0c8af');
    grad.addColorStop(1,   '#3c554b');
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
  }
  
  if (state.designImg) {
    let designPanel = null;
    let shouldDraw = false;

    // Tin rig with dieline: use the body strip (_bodyBox) as the texture instead
    // of the full image (which may include circular top-cap panels and blank areas).
    // Bottle rig: always use full image (no standard dieline format for lathe).
    if (tpl.rig === 'tin' && state.dielineMode) {
      // Crop to the horizontal body strip so only the wrap-around label
      // is mapped onto the cylinder side, not the whole page.
      const _layout = analyzeDielineLayout(state.designImg);
      const bb = _layout && _layout._bodyBox;
      if (bb && bb.w > 0 && bb.h > 0) {
        const cropCanvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        cropCanvas.width = Math.round(bb.w);
        cropCanvas.height = Math.round(bb.h);
        const cropCtx = cropCanvas.getContext('2d');
        cropCtx.drawImage(state.designImg, bb.x, bb.y, bb.w, bb.h, 0, 0, bb.w, bb.h);
        designPanel = cropCanvas;
        // Update tw/th to match the strip's proportions
        const MAX_TEX = 4096;
        const sd = Math.min(1, MAX_TEX / Math.max(bb.w, bb.h));
        tw = Math.max(4, Math.round(bb.w * sd));
        th = Math.max(4, Math.round(bb.h * sd));
        canvas.width = tw;
        canvas.height = th;
        // Redraw the metallic base at new size
        const grad2 = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
        grad2.addColorStop(0, '#7a8090'); grad2.addColorStop(0.12, '#c8cdd8');
        grad2.addColorStop(0.40, '#e8eaf0'); grad2.addColorStop(0.55, '#f5f6fa');
        grad2.addColorStop(0.72, '#d0d4de'); grad2.addColorStop(0.88, '#9aa0ae');
        grad2.addColorStop(1, '#6a7080');
        ctx.fillStyle = grad2;
        ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
      } else {
        designPanel = state.designImg;
      }
      shouldDraw = true;
    } else if (tpl.rig === 'tin' || tpl.rig === 'bottle') {
      designPanel = state.designImg;
      shouldDraw = true;
    } else if (state.dielineMode) {
      // Re-use the already-extracted panel if available
      designPanel = dielinePanel;
      if (designPanel) shouldDraw = true;
      // If dieline extraction returned nothing, fall back to the full image
      if (!designPanel && (faceName === 'front')) {
        designPanel = state.designImg;
        shouldDraw = true;
      }
    } else {
      if (faceName === 'front' || (tpl.rig === 'sachet' && faceName === 'back')) {
        designPanel = state.designImg;
        shouldDraw = true;
      }
    }
    
    if (shouldDraw && designPanel) {
      ctx.save();

      ctx.globalAlpha = 1.0;
      ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
      
      let sx = 0, sy = 0, sw = designPanel.width, sh = designPanel.height;
      let dx = 0, dy = 0, dw = tw, dh = th;
      
      if (faceName === 'top') {
        // Rotate the top panel 90° CCW to align with Three.js BoxGeometry top UVs.
        // In dieline mode tw/th are already the panel's exact pixel dims (possibly swapped
        // by the swap block below), so we just rotate the panel into the canvas.
        ctx.translate(0, th);
        ctx.rotate(-Math.PI / 2);
        // After rotation the draw space is th wide × tw tall
        ctx.drawImage(designPanel, 0, 0, designPanel.width, designPanel.height, 0, 0, th, tw);
      } else if (state.dielineMode) {
        // Texture canvas already has the exact pixel dims of this panel —
        // a direct 1:1 copy is all that's needed. Any scale-down applied when
        // the panel was > 4096px is absorbed by the canvas size, so this is lossless.
        ctx.drawImage(designPanel, 0, 0, sw, sh, 0, 0, tw, th);
      } else if (state.fit === 'stretch') {
          ctx.drawImage(designPanel, sx, sy, sw, sh, dx, dy, dw, dh);
        } else if (state.fit === 'cover') {
          const targetAR = tw / th;
          const srcAR = sw / sh;
          let cw = sw, ch = sh;
          if (srcAR > targetAR) {
            cw = sh * targetAR;
            sx = (sw - cw) / 2;
          } else {
            ch = sw / targetAR;
            sy = (sh - ch) / 2;
          }
          ctx.drawImage(designPanel, sx, sy, cw, ch, dx, dy, dw, dh);
        } else if (state.fit === 'contain') {
          const targetAR = tw / th;
          const srcAR = sw / sh;
          if (srcAR > targetAR) {
            dh = dw / srcAR;
            dy = (th - dh) / 2;
          } else {
            dw = dh * srcAR;
            dx = (tw - dw) / 2;
          }
          ctx.drawImage(designPanel, sx, sy, sw, sh, dx, dy, dw, dh);
        }
      ctx.restore();

      // ── Blend pass: apply paper/surface texture on top of design ─────────────
      // Mirrors the 2D compositor logic: draw the base cardboard/foil surface
      // using the selected blend mode so the texture modulates the design colours
      // and gives it that "printed on physical material" look.
      if (state.blend !== 'normal') {
        ctx.save();
        ctx.globalAlpha = state.opacity;
        ctx.globalCompositeOperation = state.blend === 'multiply' ? 'multiply' : 'screen';
        // Re-draw just the base material layer (paper/foil) onto the already-drawn design
        const baseLayer = document.createElement('canvas');
        baseLayer.width = tw; baseLayer.height = th;
        const blc = baseLayer.getContext('2d');
        if (tpl.rig === 'box') {
          let baseColor = '#DCD5C2';
          if (faceName === 'side' || faceName === 'other_side') baseColor = '#B8AD95';
          if (faceName === 'top') baseColor = '#EDE9DD';
          drawBasePaperTexture(blc, tw, th, baseColor);
        } else if (tpl.rig === 'sachet') {
          blc.fillStyle = '#f2efe6';
          blc.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
        } else if (tpl.rig === 'tin') {
          const grad = blc.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
          grad.addColorStop(0,    '#7a8090');
          grad.addColorStop(0.12, '#c8cdd8');
          grad.addColorStop(0.40, '#e8eaf0');
          grad.addColorStop(0.55, '#f5f6fa');
          grad.addColorStop(0.72, '#d0d4de');
          grad.addColorStop(0.88, '#9aa0ae');
          grad.addColorStop(1,    '#6a7080');
          blc.fillStyle = grad;
          blc.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
        } else if (tpl.rig === 'bottle') {
          blc.fillStyle = '#a8c4a0';
          blc.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
          const grad = blc.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
          grad.addColorStop(0,   '#506456');
          grad.addColorStop(0.20,'#82a591');
          grad.addColorStop(0.45,'#c8e6d2');
          grad.addColorStop(0.55,'#e6faeb');
          grad.addColorStop(0.75,'#a0c8af');
          grad.addColorStop(1,   '#3c554b');
          blc.fillStyle = grad;
          blc.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
        }
        ctx.drawImage(baseLayer, 0, 0);
        ctx.restore();
      }
    }
  }

  // ── Specular shading baked into texture for 3D realism ───────────────────
  // Simulates the key light (upper-left) reflecting off cardboard/foil surface.
  // Different intensity per face based on its orientation relative to light.
  if (tpl.rig) {
    ctx.save();
    let grad;
    if (faceName === 'top') {
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, th);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)');
    } else if (faceName === 'side' || faceName === 'other_side') {
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.12)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.18)');
    } else {
      // Front / back — subtle vignette
      grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, tw, 0);
      grad.addColorStop(0,   'rgba(255,255,255,0.07)');
      grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(255,255,255,0.01)');
      grad.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0.07)');
    }
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.globalCompositeOperation = 'source-over';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, tw, th);
    ctx.restore();
  }

  // NOTE: no border is baked into the texture here. The single outline you see
  // on every face comes from the EdgesGeometry wireframe added once per mesh
  // (see buildBoxMesh / the `if (geometry) {...}` block below), which already
  // draws one perspective-correct line per edge from any viewing angle,
  // including straight-down top view. Baking a second line into the texture
  // on top of that was what caused the double-border look.
  
  return canvas;
}

function clearThreeScene() {
  if (!threeScene) return;
  const toRemove = [];
  threeScene.traverse(child => {
    if (child.isMesh || child.isLine || child.isLineSegments || child.type === 'LineSegments') {
      toRemove.push(child);
    }
  });
  toRemove.forEach(obj => {
    threeScene.remove(obj);
    if (obj.geometry) obj.geometry.dispose();
    if (Array.isArray(obj.material)) {
      obj.material.forEach(mat => mat.dispose());
    } else if (obj.material) {
      obj.material.dispose();
    }
  });
}

// ── Dynamic 3D dimensions from dieline panels ────────────────────────────────
// When a dieline is loaded we know the pixel dimensions of each detected panel.
// We use these to set the Three.js BoxGeometry proportions so the texture fills
// each face perfectly with zero white bars and zero distortion.
// Falls back to template defaults when no dieline is available.
function _getDynamicBoxDims(tpl) {
  const square = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.square);
  const tube   = !!(tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.tube);

  // If the user set custom cm dimensions, convert them to Three.js units.
  // Reference scale: H=3.4 Three.js units ≈ default box height.
  const custom = state.customDimsCm[tpl.id];
  if (custom && custom.W && custom.H) {
    const refH = tube ? 2.6 : (square ? 3.7 : 3.4);
    const defCm = DIM_DEFAULTS[tpl.id] || { W:13.5, H:12.5, D:7.0 };
    const scale = refH / (defCm.H || 1);
    const W = Math.max(0.3, Math.min(12, (custom.W || defCm.W) * scale));
    const H = Math.max(0.3, Math.min(12, (custom.H || defCm.H) * scale));
    const D = Math.max(0.1, Math.min( 6, (custom.D || defCm.D) * scale));
    return { W, H, D };
  }

  // Default (template-driven) proportions
  let W = tube ? 5.5 : 3.7;
  let H = tube ? 2.6 : (square ? 3.7 : 3.4);
  let D = tube ? 0.8 : (square ? 3.7 : 1.8);

  if (state.dielineMode && state.designImg) {
    const layout = analyzeDielineLayout(state.designImg);
    const front = layout.front;
    const side  = layout.side;
    const top   = layout.top;

    if (front && front.w > 0 && front.h > 0) {
      const refH = front.h;
      const wFront = front.w;
      const wSide  = (side  && side.w  > 0) ? side.w  : (wFront * (D / W));

      // Normalise so face height = H default
      const scale = H / refH;
      W = Math.max(0.3, Math.min(12, wFront * scale));
      D = Math.max(0.1, Math.min( 6, wSide  * scale));
    }
  }

  return { W, H, D };
}

function updateThreeModel() {
  clearThreeScene();
  
  const tpl = state.template;
  let geometry;
  let materials = [];
  
  if (tpl.rig === 'box') {
    const { W: width, H: height, D: depth } = _getDynamicBoxDims(tpl);
    
    geometry = new THREE.BoxGeometry(width, height, depth);
    
    // Box faces: Right (+X), Left (-X), Top (+Y), Bottom (-Y), Front (+Z), Back (-Z)
    const faceMapping = ['side', 'other_side', 'top', 'bottom', 'front', 'back'];
    
    faceMapping.forEach((faceName, idx) => {
      let canvas = createFaceTextureCanvas(faceName, tpl);
      let texture = new THREE.CanvasTexture(canvas);
      texture.encoding = THREE.sRGBEncoding;
      texture.minFilter = THREE.LinearMipmapLinearFilter;
      texture.magFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
      texture.generateMipmaps = true;
      if (threeRenderer) {
        texture.anisotropy = threeRenderer.capabilities.getMaxAnisotropy();
      }
      
      // Per-face roughness/metalness for cardboard — top is slightly shinier
      const isTop = faceName === 'top';
      const isSide = faceName === 'side' || faceName === 'other_side';
      let mat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        map: texture,
        roughness: isTop ? 0.55 : (isSide ? 0.85 : 0.70),
        metalness: isTop ? 0.08 : 0.04,
        envMapIntensity: 0.5
      });
      materials.push(mat);
    });
    
  } else if (tpl.rig === 'sachet') {
    const width = 3.2;
    const height = 6.0;
    const depth = 0.8;
    
    // Puffed cushion geometry
    geometry = new THREE.BoxGeometry(width, height, depth, 15, 15, 1);
    
    const posAttr = geometry.attributes.position;
    for (let i = 0; i < posAttr.count; i++) {
      let x = posAttr.getX(i);
      let y = posAttr.getY(i);
      let z = posAttr.getZ(i);
      
      const nx = x / (width / 2);
      const ny = y / (height / 2);
      
      const scale = Math.cos(nx * Math.PI / 2) * Math.cos(ny * Math.PI / 2);
      posAttr.setZ(i, z * scale);
    }
    geometry.computeVertexNormals();
    
    const faceMapping = ['side', 'other_side', 'top', 'bottom', 'front', 'back'];
    
    faceMapping.forEach(faceName => {
      let canvas = createFaceTextureCanvas(faceName, tpl);
      let texture = new THREE.CanvasTexture(canvas);
      texture.encoding = THREE.sRGBEncoding;
      texture.minFilter = THREE.LinearMipmapLinearFilter;
      texture.magFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
      texture.generateMipmaps = true;
      if (threeRenderer) {
        texture.anisotropy = threeRenderer.capabilities.getMaxAnisotropy();
      }
      
      const isFront = faceName === 'front' || faceName === 'back';
      let mat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        map: texture,
        roughness: isFront ? 0.20 : 0.45,
        metalness: isFront ? 0.50 : 0.25  // Glossy foil look on face panels
      });
      materials.push(mat);
    });
  } else if (tpl.rig === 'tin' || tpl.rig === 'bottle') {
    // Use custom dimension if set, else template defaults
    const dd = tpl.defaultDims || { W:7.4, H:10.8, D:7.4 };
    const dimW = state.customDimsCm[tpl.id]?.W ?? dd.W;
    const dimH = state.customDimsCm[tpl.id]?.H ?? dd.H;

    // Normalise to a sensible Three.js unit scale (height = reference 5.5 units)
    const scale = 5.5 / dd.H;
    const cH = dimH * scale;
    const cR = (dimW / 2) * scale;

    const isSquareBottle = tpl.rig === 'bottle' && tpl.rigOpts && tpl.rigOpts.square;
    const segs = tpl.rig === 'bottle' ? 32 : 24;

    if (tpl.rig === 'tin') {
      geometry = new THREE.CylinderGeometry(cR, cR, cH, segs, 1, false);
    } else if (isSquareBottle) {
      // Square/mason-jar bottle: wide body, very short shoulder taper, short narrow neck, gold cap
      // Built as a lathe (rotationally symmetric approximation of the square body)
      const points = [];
      const neckR  = cR * 0.24;    // narrower neck relative to wide body
      const half   = cH / 2;
      const shoulderStart = -half + cH * 0.76;  // shoulder starts high (body is tall)
      const neckBot       = -half + cH * 0.84;
      const neckTop       = -half + cH * 0.92;
      // base (slightly wider) → straight body → shoulder taper → neck → cap
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR * 0.96,  -half));                 // base edge
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR,          -half + cH * 0.04));    // body starts
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR,          shoulderStart));        // body ends at shoulder
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR * 2.0, neckBot - cH * 0.02)); // shoulder taper
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR,        neckBot));             // neck bottom
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR,        neckTop));             // neck top
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR * 1.1,  half));               // cap flare
      geometry = new THREE.LatheGeometry(points, segs);
    } else {
      // Slim round bottle: lathe profile centred at y=0
      const points = [];
      const neckR = cR * 0.28;
      const half  = cH / 2;
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR * 0.95,  -half));
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR,          -half + cH * 0.10));
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(cR,          -half + cH * (1 - 0.40 - 0.22)));
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR * 1.6, -half + cH * (1 - 0.40)));
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR,        -half + cH * (1 - 0.10)));
      points.push(new THREE.Vector2(neckR,         half));
      geometry = new THREE.LatheGeometry(points, segs);
    }

    let canvas = createFaceTextureCanvas('front', tpl);
    let texture = new THREE.CanvasTexture(canvas);
    texture.encoding = THREE.sRGBEncoding;
    texture.minFilter = THREE.LinearMipmapLinearFilter;
    texture.magFilter = THREE.LinearFilter;
    texture.generateMipmaps = true;
    if (threeRenderer) texture.anisotropy = threeRenderer.capabilities.getMaxAnisotropy();

    // Tin rig: CylinderGeometry uses 3 material slots: [side, topCap, bottomCap]
    // When dieline mode is active and a top panel exists, texture the top cap.
    let capMat;
    if (tpl.rig === 'tin' && state.dielineMode && state.designImg) {
      const _layout = analyzeDielineLayout(state.designImg);
      const topPanel = _layout && (_layout.top || _layout.topBox || _layout.lid);
      if (topPanel && (topPanel.w > 0 || topPanel.canvas)) {
        // Build a square canvas for the top lid panel
        const capC = document.createElement('canvas');
        const capSz = 512;
        capC.width = capSz; capC.height = capSz;
        const capCtx = capC.getContext('2d');
        // Draw metallic silver base
        const cg = capCtx.createRadialGradient(capSz/2, capSz/2, 0, capSz/2, capSz/2, capSz/2);
        cg.addColorStop(0, '#f0f1f5'); cg.addColorStop(0.6, '#d0d4de'); cg.addColorStop(1, '#8a90a0');
        capCtx.fillStyle = cg; capCtx.fillRect(0, 0, capSz, capSz);
        // Crop the top panel from the source image and draw it centred in a circle
        const src = topPanel.canvas || state.designImg;
        const sx = topPanel.x || 0, sy = topPanel.y || 0;
        const sw = topPanel.w || src.width, sh = topPanel.h || src.height;
        const dim = Math.min(capSz * 0.92, capSz);
        const off = (capSz - dim) / 2;
        capCtx.save();
        capCtx.beginPath();
        capCtx.arc(capSz/2, capSz/2, dim/2, 0, Math.PI*2);
        capCtx.clip();
        capCtx.drawImage(src, sx, sy, sw, sh, off, off, dim, dim);
        capCtx.restore();
        const capTex = new THREE.CanvasTexture(capC);
        capTex.encoding = THREE.sRGBEncoding;
        capMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
          map: capTex, roughness: 0.35, metalness: 0.3
        });
      }
    }
    if (!capMat) {
      // Default cap: silver metallic for tin, coloured for bottle
      capMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        color: (tpl.rig === 'bottle') ? (isSquareBottle ? 0xc8a630 : 0x2d2d30) : 0xa0a8b8,
        roughness: 0.4, metalness: tpl.rig === 'tin' ? 0.55 : (isSquareBottle ? 0.7 : 0.1)
      });
    }

    if (tpl.rig === 'tin') {
      // CylinderGeometry: slot 0 = side (label), slot 1 = top cap, slot 2 = bottom cap
      let mat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        map: texture,
        roughness: 0.25, metalness: 0.45, envMapIntensity: 0.6
      });
      materials.push(mat);       // side
      materials.push(capMat);    // top cap
      materials.push(capMat);    // bottom cap
    } else {
      // Glass/bottle material — opaque with subtle glass-like finish
      let mat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({
        map: texture,
        roughness: isSquareBottle ? 0.12 : 0.18,
        metalness: isSquareBottle ? 0.08 : 0.10,
        transparent: false,
        envMapIntensity: isSquareBottle ? 0.8 : 0.5
      });
      materials.push(mat);
      materials.push(capMat);
      materials.push(capMat);
    }
  }
  
  if (geometry) {
    const meshMat = (tpl.rig === 'bottle') ? materials[0] : materials;
    threeMesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, meshMat);
    threeScene.add(threeMesh);
    
    // Single crisp border outline per edge — only for box/sachet rigs.
    // Cylindrical shapes (tin, bottle) use LatheGeometry/CylinderGeometry
    // with many segments, which creates dozens of ring-edge lines that
    // look like ugly horizontal ellipses. Skip edges for those.
    if (tpl.rig === 'box' || tpl.rig === 'sachet') {
      const edgesGeom = new THREE.EdgesGeometry(geometry, 30);
      const lineMat = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({ 
        color: 0x000000, 
        opacity: 0.35, 
        transparent: true 
      });
      const edges = new THREE.LineSegments(edgesGeom, lineMat);
      threeScene.add(edges);
    }
  }
}

function initThree() {
  if (threeRenderer) return;
  
  const threeCanvas = document.getElementById('threeCanvas');
  
  threeRenderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({
    canvas: threeCanvas,
    antialias: true,
    alpha: true,
    preserveDrawingBuffer: true
  });
  threeRenderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2));
  threeRenderer.outputEncoding = THREE.sRGBEncoding;
  threeRenderer.shadowMap.enabled = false;
  // Slight tone-mapping for a more print-accurate look
  threeRenderer.toneMapping = THREE.ACESFilmicToneMapping;
  threeRenderer.toneMappingExposure = 1.05;
  
  threeScene = new THREE.Scene();
  // Warm studio background matching the 2D canvas look
  threeScene.background = new THREE.Color(0xE5E1D8);
  
  threeCamera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(45, 1, 0.1, 100);
  threeCamera.position.set(0, 1.5, 10); // Slightly elevated view
  
  // Warm key light from upper-left (simulates studio softbox)
  const ambientLight = new THREE.AmbientLight(0xfff8f0, 0.65);
  threeScene.add(ambientLight);
  
  const keyLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xfff5e8, 0.75);
  keyLight.position.set(5, 8, 5);
  threeScene.add(keyLight);
  
  // Cool fill from opposite side
  const fillLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xe8f0ff, 0.30);
  fillLight.position.set(-5, 3, -5);
  threeScene.add(fillLight);

  // Subtle rim light from below to prevent total shadow blackness
  const rimLight = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 0.12);
  rimLight.position.set(0, -4, 3);
  threeScene.add(rimLight);
  
  threeControls = new THREE.OrbitControls(threeCamera, threeRenderer.domElement);
  threeControls.enableDamping = true;
  threeControls.dampingFactor = 0.05;
  threeControls.enablePan = false;
  threeControls.minDistance = 5;
  threeControls.maxDistance = 20;
  
  threeControls.addEventListener('change', () => {
    if (isUpdatingCamera) return;
    
    const angleRad = Math.atan2(threeCamera.position.x, threeCamera.position.z);
    let angleDeg = Math.round(angleRad * 180 / Math.PI);
    if (angleDeg < 0) angleDeg += 360;
    
    state.ttAngle = angleDeg;
    ttSlider.value = angleDeg;
    ttDeg.textContent = angleDeg + '\u00B0';
    
    updateFooter();
    threeRenderer.render(threeScene, threeCamera);
  });
}

/* =========================================================
   DIMENSION ADJUSTER
   ========================================================= */

const DIM_FIELDS = {
  box:    [ { key:'W', label:'Width'  }, { key:'H', label:'Height' }, { key:'D', label:'Depth'  } ],
  tin:    [ { key:'W', label:'Diameter'}, { key:'H', label:'Height' } ],
  bottle: [ { key:'W', label:'Diameter'}, { key:'H', label:'Height' } ],
  sachet: [ { key:'W', label:'Width'  }, { key:'H', label:'Height' }, { key:'D', label:'Depth'  } ]
};

// Default cm dimensions mirroring _getDynamicBoxDims / template defaults
const DIM_DEFAULTS = {
  'box-square-01':   { W:12.0, H:12.0, D:12.0 },
  'box-rect-01':     { W:13.5, H:12.5, D:7.0  },
  'box-tube-01':     { W:22.0, H:9.5,  D:3.0  },
  'sachet-01':       { W:8.0,  H:14.0, D:2.0  },
  'tin-can-01':      { W:7.4,  H:10.8, D:7.4  },
  'bottle-01':       { W:7.0,  H:22.0, D:7.0  },
  'bottle-square-01':{ W:8.5,  H:24.0, D:8.5  }
};

function getDimDefaults(tpl) {
  return DIM_DEFAULTS[tpl.id] || tpl.defaultDims || { W:10, H:10, D:10 };
}

function buildDimPanel(tpl) {
  const dimInputs = document.getElementById('dimInputs');
  const section   = document.getElementById('dimAdjustSection');
  const rig = tpl.rig;
  if (!rig || !DIM_FIELDS[rig]) { section.style.display = 'none'; return; }
  section.style.display = 'block';

  const fields = DIM_FIELDS[rig];
  const defaults = getDimDefaults(tpl);
  const saved = state.customDimsCm[tpl.id] || {};

  dimInputs.innerHTML = '';
  fields.forEach(({ key, label }) => {
    const val = saved[key] ?? defaults[key] ?? 10;
    const row = document.createElement('div');
    row.style.cssText = 'display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; gap:8px;';
    row.innerHTML = `
      <label style="font-size:11px; color:var(--slate-dark); min-width:60px;">${label}</label>
      <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px; flex:1;">
        <input type="number" id="dim_${key}" min="0.5" max="200" step="0.1" value="${val.toFixed(1)}"
          style="flex:1; padding:5px 8px; background:#161618; border:1px solid var(--line); border-radius:5px; color:var(--paper); font-family:var(--mono); font-size:11px; outline:none; text-align:right;">
        <span style="font-family:var(--mono); font-size:10px; color:var(--slate); width:20px;">cm</span>
      </div>
    `;
    dimInputs.appendChild(row);
  });
}

function readDimInputs(tpl) {
  const rig = tpl.rig;
  if (!rig || !DIM_FIELDS[rig]) return null;
  const result = {};
  DIM_FIELDS[rig].forEach(({ key }) => {
    const el = document.getElementById('dim_' + key);
    if (el) result[key] = Math.max(0.5, parseFloat(el.value) || 1);
  });
  return result;
}

function applyDimsToModel(silent) {
  const tpl = state.template;
  const dims = readDimInputs(tpl);
  if (!dims) return;
  state.customDimsCm[tpl.id] = dims;

  // Force Three.js cache invalidation so geometry rebuilds
  threeCache.templateId = null;

  // Also rescale pixel-corner coordinates proportionally for 2D views
  rescaleCornersFromDims(tpl, dims);

  renderStage();
  if (!silent) showToast('Dimensions applied');
}

function rescaleCornersFromDims(tpl, dims) {
  const defaults = getDimDefaults(tpl);
  const rig = tpl.rig;
  if (!rig) return;

  // ── Snapshot originals on first call so every rescale is always relative
  // to the pristine template corners, not the previously-scaled ones.
  if (!tpl._origCorners) {
    tpl._origCorners = tpl.corners.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl.cornersFront)     tpl._origCornersFront     = tpl.cornersFront.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl.cornersTop)       tpl._origCornersTop       = tpl.cornersTop.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl.cornersSide)      tpl._origCornersSide      = tpl.cornersSide.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl.cornersBack)      tpl._origCornersBack      = tpl.cornersBack.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl.cornersOtherSide) tpl._origCornersOtherSide = tpl.cornersOtherSide.map(p => p.slice());
  }

  if (rig === 'box') {
    const scaleW = dims.W / (defaults.W || 1);
    const scaleH = dims.H / (defaults.H || 1);
    const [cw, ch] = tpl.canvas;
    const cx = cw / 2, cy = ch / 2;
    const scaleCorners = (arr) => arr.map(([x, y]) => [
      Math.round(cx + (x - cx) * scaleW),
      Math.round(cy + (y - cy) * scaleH)
    ]);
    // Always rebase from the original (unmodified) corners
    tpl.corners          = scaleCorners(tpl._origCorners);
    if (tpl._origCornersFront)     tpl.cornersFront     = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersFront);
    if (tpl._origCornersTop)       tpl.cornersTop       = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersTop);
    if (tpl._origCornersSide)      tpl.cornersSide      = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersSide);
    if (tpl._origCornersBack)      tpl.cornersBack      = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersBack);
    if (tpl._origCornersOtherSide) tpl.cornersOtherSide = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersOtherSide);
    updateCornersForView();
  } else if (rig === 'tin' || rig === 'bottle') {
    const scaleW = dims.W / (defaults.W || 1);
    const scaleH = dims.H / (defaults.H || 1);
    const [cw, ch] = tpl.canvas;
    const cx = cw / 2, cy = ch / 2;
    const scaleCorners = (arr) => arr.map(([x, y]) => [
      Math.round(cx + (x - cx) * scaleW),
      Math.round(cy + (y - cy) * scaleH)
    ]);
    tpl.corners = scaleCorners(tpl._origCorners);
    if (tpl._origCornersFront) tpl.cornersFront = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersFront);
    if (tpl._origCornersTop)   tpl.cornersTop   = scaleCorners(tpl._origCornersTop);
    updateCornersForView();
  }
}

function matchAspectRatio() {
  if (!state.designImg) return;
  const tpl = state.template;
  const rig = tpl.rig;
  if (!rig) return;

  const defaults = getDimDefaults(tpl);
  const currentDims = readDimInputs(tpl) || defaults;
  const newDims = { ...currentDims };

  if (rig === 'tin') {
    // For a cylinder: circumference = π × D, and we want (π × D) / H = bodyW / bodyH
    // so D = (bodyW × H) / (π × bodyH)
    // In dieline mode, use the _bodyBox strip (the actual wrap-around label band);
    // otherwise fall back to the full image ratio.
    let bodyAR = null;
    if (state.dielineMode) {
      const _layout = analyzeDielineLayout(state.designImg);
      const bb = _layout && _layout._bodyBox;
      if (bb && bb.w > 0 && bb.h > 0) {
        bodyAR = bb.w / bb.h;  // width-to-height of the wrap strip
      }
    }
    if (bodyAR === null) {
      // No dieline / no bodyBox: use full image ratio
      const img = state.designImg;
      const iw = img.naturalWidth || img.width;
      const ih = img.naturalHeight || img.height;
      if (!iw || !ih) return;
      bodyAR = iw / ih;
    }
    // D = (bodyAR × H) / π  →  diameter that makes the label wrap exactly once
    newDims.W = parseFloat(((bodyAR * currentDims.H) / Math.PI).toFixed(1));
    newDims.W = Math.max(1, Math.min(60, newDims.W));

  } else if (rig === 'bottle') {
    const img = state.designImg;
    const iw = img.naturalWidth || img.width;
    const ih = img.naturalHeight || img.height;
    if (!iw || !ih) return;
    newDims.W = parseFloat(((iw / ih * currentDims.H) / Math.PI).toFixed(1));
    newDims.W = Math.max(1, Math.min(60, newDims.W));

  } else if (rig === 'box' || rig === 'sachet') {
    const img = state.designImg;
    const iw = img.naturalWidth || img.width;
    const ih = img.naturalHeight || img.height;
    if (!iw || !ih) return;
    newDims.W = parseFloat((currentDims.H * (iw / ih)).toFixed(1));
  }

  const wEl = document.getElementById('dim_W');
  if (wEl) wEl.value = newDims.W.toFixed(1);

  state.customDimsCm[tpl.id] = { ...currentDims, W: newDims.W };
  threeCache.templateId = null;
  rescaleCornersFromDims(tpl, state.customDimsCm[tpl.id]);
  renderStage();
}

document.getElementById('applyDimsBtn').addEventListener('click', applyDimsToModel);
document.getElementById('resetDimsBtn').addEventListener('click', () => {
  const tpl = state.template;
  delete state.customDimsCm[tpl.id];
  threeCache.templateId = null;

  // Restore corners to their true originals (if we ever snapshotted them)
  if (tpl._origCorners) {
    tpl.corners = tpl._origCorners.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl._origCornersFront)     tpl.cornersFront     = tpl._origCornersFront.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl._origCornersTop)       tpl.cornersTop       = tpl._origCornersTop.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl._origCornersSide)      tpl.cornersSide      = tpl._origCornersSide.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl._origCornersBack)      tpl.cornersBack      = tpl._origCornersBack.map(p => p.slice());
    if (tpl._origCornersOtherSide) tpl.cornersOtherSide = tpl._origCornersOtherSide.map(p => p.slice());
    updateCornersForView();
  }

  buildDimPanel(tpl);
  renderStage();
  showToast('Dimensions reset');
});

// Update dim panel whenever template changes (hook into selectTemplate via MutationObserver on stageTplName)
const _origSelectTemplate = selectTemplate;
// (selectTemplate already calls renderStage; we patch the call at the bottom)

/* =========================================================
   INIT
   ========================================================= */
renderTemplateGrid();
selectTemplate(state.template.id);
buildDimPanel(state.template);
// Rebuild dim panel whenever a new template is selected
const _tplGrid = document.getElementById('tplGrid');
_tplGrid.addEventListener('click', () => {
  // After selectTemplate fires (next microtask)
  setTimeout(() => buildDimPanel(state.template), 0);
});
window.addEventListener('resize', renderStage);


</script>

<!-- PAGE 5: AI PROMPT STUDIO — Free AI Mockup Generation (No API Key Required) -->

</div><!-- /app -->

<!-- TAB NAVIGATION — placed here so ALL pages exist in DOM before querySelectorAll runs -->
<script>
(function(){
  const nav = document.getElementById('tabNav');
  const tabs = nav.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn');

  function switchTab(targetId) {
    const pages = document.querySelectorAll('.page');
    tabs.forEach(t => t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.page === targetId));
    pages.forEach(p => {
      const isTarget = p.id === targetId;
      // Always remove active first, reset display to none
      p.classList.remove('active');
      p.style.display = 'none';
      p.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
      if (isTarget) {
        p.classList.add('active');
        p.style.display = '';      // Let CSS .active rule take over
        p.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
      }
    });
    if (targetId === 'page-mockup') {
      setTimeout(renderStage, 50);
    }

  }

  tabs.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => switchTab(btn.dataset.page));
  });

  // Expose globally so key status badge can link to GenMock
  window.switchTab = switchTab;

  // Initial state — ensure only mockup page visible
  switchTab('page-mockup');
})();
</script>

</body>
